## FR-PROD-051 文件缩略图生成

**需求描述**：上传后自动生成缩略图（PDF转缩略图），命名规则为原文件名加 `_thumb` 后缀。

**Controller**：缩略图生成由异步Job处理，无直接Controller接口。

**Job**：
```php
class GenerateThumbnailJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(private readonly int $orderFileId)
    {
    }

    public function handle(FileMetadataExtractorService $fileMetaService): void
    {
        $orderFile = OrderFile::findOrFail($this->orderFileId);

        // 下载文件到临时路径
        $tempPath = $this->downloadToTemp($orderFile->file_url);
        $uploadedFile = new UploadedFile($tempPath, $orderFile->file_name);

        // 检测格式
        $format = $fileMetaService->detectFormat($uploadedFile);

        // 生成缩略图
        $thumbUrl = $fileMetaService->generateThumbnail($uploadedFile, $format);

        // 更新记录
        $orderFile->update([
            'thumbnail_url' => $thumbUrl,
        ]);

        // 清理临时文件
        @unlink($tempPath);
    }
}
```

**Service**：`FileMetadataExtractorService::generateThumbnail()`（已在 `supplement_product.md` 6.42.6 节定义）

**命名规则**：缩略图URL由原文件名加 `_thumb` 后缀生成，如 `design.pdf` → `design_thumb.jpg`。

---

## FR-PROD-052 直传OSS

**需求描述**：前端直接将文件上传至阿里云OSS/MinIO。

**Controller**：无直接Controller，前端通过OSS SDK直传。

**流程**：
1. 前端调用后端获取临时STS凭证：`GET /api/Oss/StsToken`
2. 前端直传文件到OSS/MinIO
3. 前端获取OSS返回的URL
4. 前端调用 `POST /api/WebOrderFiles/ConfirmUpload` 确认上传

**配置**：
```php
// config/services.php
'oss' => [
    'access_key_id' => env('OSS_ACCESS_KEY_ID'),
    'access_key_secret' => env('OSS_ACCESS_KEY_SECRET'),
    'endpoint' => env('OSS_ENDPOINT'),
    'bucket' => env('OSS_BUCKET'),
    'domain' => env('OSS_DOMAIN', 'https://web-oss.sd2000.com/pisweb/'),
],
```

---

## FR-PROD-052-A 文件上传确认

**需求描述**：前端直传OSS成功后，必须调用确认接口通知后端文件已上传，后端记录文件URL、大小、类型等元数据。

**Controller**：`OrderController::confirmUpload()`（见FR-PROD-043）

**路由**：`POST /api/WebOrderFiles/ConfirmUpload`

**说明**：此接口为文件上传流程的必要步骤，OSS直传成功但不调用确认接口则文件不被系统识别。

---

## FR-PROD-052-B 上传失败补偿

**需求描述**：若OSS直传成功但确认接口调用失败，前端应在30秒内自动重试3次；超过3次仍失败则标记为"上传异常"，提示用户重新上传。后端提供兜底补偿机制，定时扫描未确认上传记录并自动重试或标记异常。

**前端实现**：
```typescript
// 前端重试逻辑
async function confirmUploadWithRetry(params: ConfirmUploadParams): Promise<void> {
    const maxRetries = 3;
    const retryInterval = 10000; // 10秒

    for (let i = 0; i < maxRetries; i++) {
        try {
            await api.post('/api/WebOrderFiles/ConfirmUpload', params);
            return;
        } catch (error) {
            if (i === maxRetries - 1) {
                // 标记上传异常
                await api.post('/api/WebOrderFiles/MarkUploadException', {
                    ...params,
                    error: error.message,
                });
                throw new Error('上传异常，请重新上传');
            }
            await sleep(retryInterval);
        }
    }
}
```

**后端兜底机制**：

### 数据表：`upload_confirm_retries`

| 字段 | 类型 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| `id` | bigint PK | 自增主键 |
| `oss_key` | string(500) | OSS文件唯一标识 |
| `file_name` | string(255) | 原始文件名 |
| `file_size` | bigint | 文件大小（字节） |
| `file_type` | string(50) | 文件MIME类型 |
| `order_id` | bigint nullable | 关联订单ID |
| `brand_id` | bigint | 关联品牌ID |
| `customer_id` | bigint | 上传用户ID |
| `retry_count` | tinyint default 0 | 已重试次数 |
| `status` | tinyint default 0 | 0=待处理, 1=已确认, 2=异常, 3=孤儿文件 |
| `created_at` | timestamp | 创建时间 |
| `confirmed_at` | timestamp nullable | 确认成功时间 |
| `exception_reason` | string(500) nullable | 异常原因 |

```php
<?php

use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schema;

return new class extends Migration
{
    public function up(): void
    {
        Schema::create('upload_confirm_retries', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id();
            $table->string('oss_key', 500)->index()->comment('OSS文件唯一标识');
            $table->string('file_name', 255)->comment('原始文件名');
            $table->unsignedBigInteger('file_size')->comment('文件大小（字节）');
            $table->string('file_type', 50)->comment('文件MIME类型');
            $table->foreignId('order_id')->nullable()->constrained('orders')->comment('关联订单ID');
            $table->foreignId('brand_id')->constrained('brands')->comment('关联品牌ID');
            $table->foreignId('customer_id')->constrained('customers')->comment('上传用户ID');
            $table->unsignedTinyInteger('retry_count')->default(0)->comment('已重试次数');
            $table->unsignedTinyInteger('status')->default(0)->comment('0=待处理,1=已确认,2=异常,3=孤儿文件');
            $table->timestamp('confirmed_at')->nullable()->comment('确认成功时间');
            $table->string('exception_reason', 500)->nullable()->comment('异常原因');
            $table->timestamps();

            $table->index(['status', 'created_at']);
        });
    }

    public function down(): void
    {
        Schema::dropIfExists('upload_confirm_retries');
    }
};
```

### Service：`UploadConfirmRetryService`

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services;

use App\Models\UploadConfirmRetry;
use App\Jobs\ConfirmUploadJob;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class UploadConfirmRetryService
{
    /**
     * 创建待确认上传记录（OSS直传成功后、确认接口调用前插入）
     */
    public function createPendingRecord(array $data): UploadConfirmRetry
    {
        return UploadConfirmRetry::create([
            'oss_key'     => $data['oss_key'],
            'file_name'   => $data['file_name'],
            'file_size'   => $data['file_size'],
            'file_type'   => $data['file_type'],
            'order_id'    => $data['order_id'] ?? null,
            'brand_id'    => $data['brand_id'],
            'customer_id' => $data['customer_id'],
            'status'      => 0,
            'retry_count' => 0,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 确认成功时更新记录
     */
    public function markConfirmed(string $ossKey): void
    {
        UploadConfirmRetry::where('oss_key', $ossKey)
            ->update(['status' => 1, 'confirmed_at' => now()]);
    }

    /**
     * 获取超30秒未确认的记录
     */
    public function getPendingRecords(int $minutes = 1): array
    {
        return UploadConfirmRetry::where('status', 0)
            ->where('created_at', '<=', now()->subSeconds(30))
            ->where('retry_count', '<', 3)
            ->get()
            ->all();
    }

    /**
     * 执行后端补偿重试
     */
    public function processRetry(UploadConfirmRetry $record): void
    {
        try {
            $record->increment('retry_count');

            // 调用确认接口内部逻辑
            $confirmed = app(OrderFileService::class)->confirmUpload([
                'oss_key'     => $record->oss_key,
                'file_name'   => $record->file_name,
                'file_size'   => $record->file_size,
                'file_type'   => $record->file_type,
                'order_id'    => $record->order_id,
                'brand_id'    => $record->brand_id,
                'customer_id' => $record->customer_id,
            ]);

            if ($confirmed) {
                $this->markConfirmed($record->oss_key);
                Log::info('[UploadConfirmRetry] 后端补偿确认成功', ['oss_key' => $record->oss_key]);
            } else {
                throw new \RuntimeException('确认接口返回失败');
            }
        } catch (\Throwable $e) {
            Log::warning('[UploadConfirmRetry] 后端补偿重试失败', [
                'oss_key' => $record->oss_key,
                'retry_count' => $record->retry_count,
                'error' => $e->getMessage(),
            ]);

            if ($record->retry_count >= 3) {
                $record->update([
                    'status' => 2,
                    'exception_reason' => '后端补偿重试3次仍失败: ' . $e->getMessage(),
                ]);
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * 清理超过24小时仍未确认的孤儿文件
     */
    public function cleanOrphanFiles(): int
    {
        $orphans = UploadConfirmRetry::whereIn('status', [0, 2])
            ->where('created_at', '<=', now()->subHours(24))
            ->get();

        $count = 0;
        foreach ($orphans as $record) {
            try {
                // 删除OSS上的孤儿文件
                app(FileStorageService::class)->delete($record->oss_key);
                $record->update(['status' => 3]);
                $count++;
            } catch (\Throwable $e) {
                Log::error('[UploadConfirmRetry] 清理孤儿文件失败', [
                    'oss_key' => $record->oss_key,
                    'error' => $e->getMessage(),
                ]);
            }
        }

        return $count;
    }
}
```

### Console Command：`ProcessPendingUploadConfirmations`

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use App\Services\UploadConfirmRetryService;
use Illuminate\Console\Command;

class ProcessPendingUploadConfirmations extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'upload:process-pending-confirmations';
    protected $description = '扫描并处理超30秒未确认的上传记录，执行后端补偿重试';

    public function handle(UploadConfirmRetryService $service): int
    {
        $records = $service->getPendingRecords();

        if (empty($records)) {
            $this->info('没有待处理的未确认上传记录');
            return self::SUCCESS;
        }

        $this->info(sprintf('发现 %d 条待处理记录', count($records)));

        foreach ($records as $record) {
            $service->processRetry($record);
            $this->info(sprintf('已处理: %s (重试次数: %d)', $record->oss_key, $record->retry_count));
        }

        // 同时清理超过24小时的孤儿文件
        $cleaned = $service->cleanOrphanFiles();
        if ($cleaned > 0) {
            $this->info(sprintf('已清理 %d 个孤儿文件', $cleaned));
        }

        return self::SUCCESS;
    }
}
```

### 定时任务配置（Kernel.php）

```php
// app/Console/Kernel.php
protected function schedule(Schedule $schedule): void
{
    // 每5分钟扫描一次未确认上传记录
    $schedule->command('upload:process-pending-confirmations')
        ->everyFiveMinutes()
        ->withoutOverlapping()
        ->appendOutputTo(storage_path('logs/upload-confirm-retry.log'));
}
```

### 更新后的上传流程

1. **前端OSS直传成功** → 先调用 `UploadConfirmRetryService::createPendingRecord()` 创建待确认记录
2. **调用确认接口** → 成功则 `markConfirmed()` 更新状态为已确认
3. **确认接口失败** → 前端按原有逻辑重试3次
4. **后端兜底** → 定时任务每5分钟扫描 `status=0` 且 `created_at <= 30秒前` 的记录，自动执行补偿重试最多3次
5. **最终失败** → 标记为异常状态（2），前端可在列表中查询到异常文件并提示重新上传
6. **孤儿文件清理** → 超过24小时仍未确认的，自动删除OSS文件并标记为孤儿文件（3）

**说明**：此设计确保即使前端重试全部失败，后端仍能通过定时任务完成兜底补偿，同时避免OSS存储空间被孤儿文件无限占用。

## FR-PROD-056 单文件大小限制（500MB）

```php
class OrderController extends Controller
{
    public function confirmUpload(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $validated = $request->validate([
            'files' => 'required|array',
            'files.*.size' => [
                'required',
                'integer',
                'max:524288000', // FR-PROD-056: 500MB = 524,288,000 bytes
            ],
        ]);

        // ... 后续处理
    }
}
```

**路由**：`POST /api/WebOrderFiles/ConfirmUpload`

**前端校验**：
```typescript
const MAX_FILE_SIZE = 500 * 1024 * 1024; // 500MB
if (file.size > MAX_FILE_SIZE) {
    throw new Error(`文件大小超过限制：最大500MB，当前 ${(file.size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2)}MB`);
}
```

## FR-PROD-057 批量上传

**需求描述**：支持同时上传多个文件。

**Controller**：
```php
class OrderController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * FR-PROD-057: 批量上传确认
     */
    public function confirmUpload(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $validated = $request->validate([
            'order_sn' => 'required|string',
            'files' => 'required|array|max:50', // 最多50个文件
            'files.*.url' => 'required|string|url',
            'files.*.name' => 'required|string',
            'files.*.size' => 'required|integer|max:524288000',
            'files.*.mime_type' => 'required|string',
        ]);

        $order = Order::where('sn', $validated['order_sn'])->firstOrFail();
        $savedFiles = [];

        foreach ($validated['files'] as $fileMeta) {
            $savedFiles[] = OrderFile::create([
                'order_id' => $order->id,
                'file_name' => $fileMeta['name'],
                'file_url' => $fileMeta['url'],
                'file_size' => $fileMeta['size'],
                'mime_type' => $fileMeta['mime_type'],
            ]);
        }

        return $this->success([
            'uploaded_count' => count($savedFiles),
            'files' => OrderFileResource::collection($savedFiles),
        ]);
    }
}
```

**路由**：`POST /api/WebOrderFiles/ConfirmUpload`

**参数**：`files: FileMeta[]` 数组，每个元素含 `url`, `name`, `size`, `mime_type`。

// OrderController::confirmUpload
foreach ($savedFiles as $file) {
    GenerateThumbnailJob::dispatch($file->id); // FR-PROD-058
}

## FR-PROD-059 文件信息提取

**需求描述**：自动提取页数、尺寸、颜色模式、分辨率等元数据。

**Service**：
```php
class FileMetadataExtractorService
{
    /**
     * FR-PROD-059: 文件信息提取
     */
    public function extract(UploadedFile $file, FileFormat $format): array
    {
        $meta = [
            'width_px' => null,
            'height_px' => null,
            'width_mm' => null,
            'height_mm' => null,
            'dpi' => null,
            'color_mode' => null,
            'page_count' => null,
        ];

        // 位图/PDF统一使用Imagick提取
        if ($format->isRaster() || $format === FileFormat::PDF) {
            $meta = array_merge($meta, $this->extractWithImagick($file));
        }

        // PDF额外提取页数
        if ($format === FileFormat::PDF) {
            $meta['page_count'] = $this->extractPdfPageCount($file);
        }

        return $meta;
    }
}
```

**路由**：内部服务调用，无直接API。

**调用点**：`OrderController::confirmUpload` → `ValidateDesignFileAction` → `FileMetadataExtractorService::extract()`

---

## FR-PROD-060 文件校验

**需求描述**：检查文件完整性、格式正确性、是否损坏。

**Service（新增）**：
```php
class FileValidationService
{
    /**
     * FR-PROD-060: 文件完整性校验
     */
    public function validate(UploadedFile $file, FileFormat $format): array
    {
        $errors = [];

        // 1. 文件大小校验
        if ($file->getSize() === 0) {
            $errors[] = '文件大小为0，可能上传失败';
        }

        // 2. 格式一致性校验
        $detectedFormat = app(FileMetadataExtractorService::class)->detectFormat($file);
        if ($detectedFormat !== $format) {
            $errors[] = "文件扩展名与内容格式不一致：扩展名 {$format->label()}，实际 {$detectedFormat->label()}";
        }

        // 3. 文件损坏检测
        try {
            match ($format) {
                FileFormat::PDF => $this->validatePdf($file),
                FileFormat::JPG, FileFormat::PNG, FileFormat::TIFF => $this->validateImage($file),
                default => true,
            };
        } catch (\Exception $e) {
            $errors[] = '文件可能已损坏：' . $e->getMessage();
        }

        return $errors;
    }

    private function validatePdf(UploadedFile $file): void
    {
        $content = file_get_contents($file->getRealPath(), false, null, 0, 8);
        if (! str_starts_with($content, '%PDF')) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('PDF文件头异常');
        }
    }

    private function validateImage(UploadedFile $file): void
    {
        if (! getimagesize($file->getRealPath())) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('图片文件无法解析');
        }
    }
}
```

**调用点**：`OrderController::confirmUpload` → `FileValidationService::validate()`

---

## FR-PROD-061 墨量预检

**需求描述**：分析设计稿墨量分布，预警高墨量区域。

**Service（新增）**：
```php
class InkCoverageService
{
    /**
     * FR-PROD-061: 墨量预检分析
     */
    public function analyze(string $filePath, FileFormat $format): array
    {
        $result = [
            'total_coverage' => 0,    // 总墨量覆盖率 %
            'cmyk_coverage' => [       // 分色墨量
                'c' => 0, 'm' => 0, 'y' => 0, 'k' => 0,
            ],
            'high_risk_areas' => [],   // 高墨量区域坐标
            'warning' => false,        // 是否预警
        ];

        if ($format !== FileFormat::PDF) {
            return $result; // 仅支持PDF墨量分析
        }

        $imagick = new Imagick();
        $imagick->setResolution(150, 150);
        $imagick->readImage($filePath);

        $totalPixels = $imagick->getImageWidth() * $imagick->getImageHeight();
        $histogram = $imagick->getImageHistogram();

        // 计算总墨量（CMYK各通道平均值）
        $inkTotal = 0;
        foreach ($histogram as $pixel) {
            $color = $pixel->getColor();
            $inkTotal += (1 - $color['r'] / 65535) * $pixel->getColorCount();
        }

        $result['total_coverage'] = round(($inkTotal / $totalPixels) * 100, 2);
        $result['warning'] = $result['total_coverage'] > 300; // 总墨量>300%预警

        $imagick->clear();

        return $result;
    }
}
```

**Job**：`InkCoverageCheckJob`（见FR-PROD-037）

**调用点**：`OrderController::confirmUpload` 异步触发 `InkCoverageCheckJob`

## FR-PROD-063 文件版本管理

**需求描述**：同一订单多次上传文件时保留历史版本。

**Controller**：
```php
class OrderController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * FR-PROD-063: 文件版本管理
     */
    private function getNextFileVersion(int $orderId, string $fileName): int
    {
        $latest = OrderFile::where('order_id', $orderId)
            ->where('file_name', $fileName)
            ->max('version');

        return ($latest ?? 0) + 1;
    }

    public function confirmUpload(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        // ... 创建文件时
        OrderFile::create([
            'version' => $this->getNextFileVersion($order->id, $fileMeta['name']),
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 获取文件版本历史
     */
    public function fileVersions(Request $request, int $fileId): JsonResponse
    {
        $file = OrderFile::findOrFail($fileId);
        $versions = OrderFile::where('order_id', $file->order_id)
            ->where('file_name', $file->file_name)
            ->orderByDesc('version')
            ->get();

        return $this->success(['versions' => OrderFileResource::collection($versions)]);
    }
}
```

**路由**：`POST /api/WebOrderFiles/ConfirmUpload` / `GET /api/WebOrderFiles/{fileId}/Versions`

**Migration**：
```php
Schema::table('order_files', function (Blueprint $table) {
    $table->integer('version')->default(1)->comment('文件版本号');
});
```

## FR-PROD-065 生产前文件锁定

**需求描述**：订单进入"生产中"状态后，文件不可修改。

**Policy**：
```php
class OrderFilePolicy
{
    /**
     * FR-PROD-065: 生产前文件锁定
     */
    public function update(User $user, OrderFile $orderFile): bool
    {
        $order = $orderFile->order;

        // 订单状态 >= 3（生产中）时禁止修改文件
        if ($order->status >= OrderStatus::PRODUCING->value) {
            return false;
        }

        return $order->customer_id === $user->id;
    }

    public function delete(User $user, OrderFile $orderFile): bool
    {
        return $this->update($user, $orderFile);
    }
}
```

**Controller**：
```php
class OrderController extends Controller
{
    public function batchRemoveFiles(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $order = Order::where('sn', $validated['order_sn'])->firstOrFail();

        // FR-PROD-065
        if ($order->status >= OrderStatus::PRODUCING->value) {
            return $this->error('订单已进入生产中，文件不可删除', 403);
        }

        // ... 删除逻辑
    }
}
```

**路由**：`POST /api/WebOrderFiles/BatchRemove`

---

## FR-PROD-066 文件归档策略

**需求描述**：订单完成后按客户ID+订单号归档，保留期限可配置。

**Command**：
```php
class FileArchive extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'file:archive {--dry-run}';
    protected $description = 'FR-PROD-066: 归档已完成订单文件';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $retentionDays = config('services.file.retention_days', 365);
        $cutoffDate = now()->subDays($retentionDays);

        $orders = Order::where('status', OrderStatus::COMPLETED->value)
            ->where('updated_at', '<', $cutoffDate)
            ->where('files_archived', false)
            ->cursor();

        foreach ($orders as $order) {
            $archivePath = "archives/{$order->customer_id}/{$order->sn}";

            foreach ($order->files as $file) {
                $this->fileService->moveToArchive($file->file_url, $archivePath);
            }

            $order->update(['files_archived' => true]);
            $this->info("已归档订单 {$order->sn}");
        }

        return 0;
    }
}
```

**执行**：`php artisan file:archive`

**定时任务**：
```php
// routes/console.php
Schedule::command('file:archive')->dailyAt('02:00');
```

**配置**：
```php
// config/services.php
'file' => [
    'retention_days' => env('FILE_RETENTION_DAYS', 365),
    'archive_bucket' => env('FILE_ARCHIVE_BUCKET', 'archive'),
],
```

## FR-PROD-068 3D模型加载

**需求描述**：支持加载Three.js格式的3D模型文件，自动适配不同产品品类；提供 `/three/form` 路由用于3D模型表单配置。

**Controller（新增）**：
```php
class ProductController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * FR-PROD-068: 3D模型加载
     */
    public function load3DModel(int $id): JsonResponse
    {
        $product = Product::with('category')->findOrFail($id);

        // 查询3D模型配置
        $modelConfig = Product3DModel::where('product_id', $id)
            ->orWhere('category_id', $product->category_id)
            ->first();

        if (! $modelConfig) {
            return $this->error('该商品暂无3D模型', 404);
        }

        return $this->success([
            'model_url' => $modelConfig->model_url,         // .glb / .gltf 文件URL
            'texture_url' => $modelConfig->texture_url,     // 贴图URL
            'config' => [
                'auto_rotate' => $modelConfig->auto_rotate ?? true,
                'camera_position' => $modelConfig->camera_position ?? [0, 0, 5],
                'light_intensity' => $modelConfig->light_intensity ?? 1.0,
                'background_color' => $modelConfig->background_color ?? '#f5f5f5',
            ],
            'hotspots' => $modelConfig->hotspots ?? [],     // 热点标注
            'adaptive_params' => $this->getAdaptiveParams($product), // 按品类自适应
        ]);
    }

    private function getAdaptiveParams(Product $product): array
    {
        return match ($product->category->cd_category_id) {
            'MINGPIAN' => ['default_scale' => [1, 0.6, 0.01], 'up_axis' => 'Z'],
            'HUACE' => ['default_scale' => [1, 1.4, 0.05], 'up_axis' => 'Z'],
            'SHUXINGHE' => ['default_scale' => [1, 1, 1], 'up_axis' => 'Y'],
            default => ['default_scale' => [1, 1, 1], 'up_axis' => 'Y'],
        };
    }
}
```

**路由**：`GET /api/Common/3DModel/{id}`

**前端路由**：`/three/form`

**Migration**：`product_3d_models` 表
```php
Schema::create('product_3d_models', function (Blueprint $table) {
    $table->id();
    $table->foreignId('product_id')->nullable()->constrained('products');
    $table->foreignId('category_id')->nullable()->constrained('product_categories');
    $table->string('model_url', 500)->comment('3D模型文件URL(.glb/.gltf)');
    $table->string('texture_url', 500)->nullable()->comment('贴图URL');
    $table->json('camera_position')->nullable();
    $table->float('light_intensity')->default(1.0);
    $table->string('background_color', 16)->default('#f5f5f5');
    $table->json('hotspots')->nullable()->comment('热点标注 [{x,y,z,label}]');
    $table->boolean('auto_rotate')->default(true);
    $table->timestamps();
});
```

# 8.12 订单/购物车/支付/物流系统缺失FR完整设计映射

> **文档定位**：本章节作为《怡安印刷商城-系统设计方案_PHP8.5_Laravel13.md》的独立补充文件，针对 `supplement_core_fr_mapping.md` 审查结果中标识为 **⚠️ 缺失 / ⚠️ 重点检查项** 的FR，补充完整的 Controller/Action/Service/Job/Request/Resource 设计。
> 
> **覆盖范围**：
> - 模块四：购物车（FR-CART-001 ~ FR-CART-009）
> - 模块五：订单系统（FR-ORDER-021 ~ FR-ORDER-058，聚焦取消/定金/来源/位掩码）
> - 模块六：支付系统（FR-PAY-022, FR-PAY-025 ~ FR-PAY-027, FR-PAY-029）
> - 模块七：物流与配送（FR-LOG-031, FR-LOG-034, FR-LOG-035）
>
> **技术栈**：PHP 8.5 + Laravel 13.x
> **设计原则**：薄控制器（Thin Controller）、Action原子化、FormRequest校验解耦、Resource响应标准化、状态机内聚。

---

## 1. 模块四：购物车系统（FR-CART-001~009）

> **审查结论**：FR-CART-001~009 全部缺失 SDD 映射，但 `CartController` 骨架已存在（`add/list/update/delete/clear` 方法）。本节补全完整设计，包括 Action、Service、FormRequest、Resource、路由。

### 1.1 数据模型设计

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Models;

use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Factories\HasFactory;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Model;
use Illuminate\Database\Eloquent\Relations\BelongsTo;

> ⚠️ **FIX-P0-1/P0-2**: 以下设计C（单表Cart Model）已废弃。统一使用主文档5.2.23节和6.2.3.1节的 `Cart` + `CartItem` 双表Model。

```php
// 废弃设计C（单表Cart），请勿使用
// class Cart extends Model { ... }
```

** carts + cart_items 表结构（唯一有效版本）**

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 |
|--------|------|------|
| **carts 表** |
| `id` | BIGINT UNSIGNED PK | 自增ID |
| `customer_id` | BIGINT UNSIGNED | 客户ID（登录后），可空 |
| `session_id` | VARCHAR(64) | 匿名会话ID（未登录），可空 |
| `status` | TINYINT | 1=正常 0=废弃 |
| `expire_at` | TIMESTAMP | 购物车整体过期时间 |
| **cart_items 表** |
| `id` | BIGINT UNSIGNED PK | 自增ID |
| `cart_id` | BIGINT UNSIGNED | 购物车ID |
| `product_id` | BIGINT UNSIGNED | 商品ID |
| `category_id` | BIGINT UNSIGNED | 品类ID（冗余，用于统计） |
| `cp_summary` | VARCHAR(512) | 参数摘要（业务级规格唯一标识） |
| `param_snapshot` | JSON | 参数选择快照（完整JSON） |
| `quantity` | INT | 数量 |
| `unit_price` | INT | 单价（单位：分） |
| `total_price` | INT | 小计 = 单价 × 数量（单位：分） |
| `file_ids` | JSON | 关联设计文件ID列表 |
| `brand_id` | BIGINT UNSIGNED | 品牌ID |
| `remark` | VARCHAR(255) | 备注/失效原因 |
| `is_selected` | TINYINT(1) | 是否选中，默认1 |
| `is_urgent` | TINYINT(1) | 是否加急，默认0 |
| `status` | TINYINT | 1=有效 0=失效 |
| `expire_at` | TIMESTAMP | 单项过期时间 |

**索引**：`uk_cart_item_spec` (`cart_id`, `product_id`, `cp_summary`) 唯一索引，替代原 `spec_hash`。

---

### 1.2 枚举定义

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 购物车操作类型
 */
enum CartOperationType: string
{
    case ADD      = 'add';
    case UPDATE   = 'update';
    case DELETE   = 'delete';
    case SELECT   = 'select';
    case UNSELECT = 'unselect';
    case CLEAR    = 'clear';
}
```

### 1.3 Service 层设计

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services;

use App\Models\Cart;
use App\Models\Customer;
use App\Models\Product;
use Illuminate\Support\Collection;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

/**
 * 购物车服务
 * 封装购物车核心业务逻辑：添加、更新、计算、选中状态管理
 */
class CartService
{
    private const int CART_MAX_ITEMS = 50;
    private const int CART_EXPIRE_DAYS = 30;

    public function __construct(
        private PricingService $pricingService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 添加商品到购物车
     * FR-CART-001, FR-CART-002
     *
     * FIX-P0-2: spec_snapshot/spec_hash → cp_summary/param_snapshot
     * FIX-P0-1: 单表 → 双表（carts + cart_items）
     */
    public function add(
        int $customerId,
        int $productId,
        string $cpSummary,
        array $paramSnapshot,
        int $quantity,
        ?array $fileIds = null,
        ?int $brandId = null,
        bool $isUrgent = false,
    ): CartItem {
        $product = Product::findOrFail($productId);

        return DB::transaction(function () use (
            $customerId, $product, $cpSummary, $paramSnapshot,
            $quantity, $fileIds, $brandId, $isUrgent
        ) {
            $cart = Cart::firstOrCreate(
                ['customer_id' => $customerId],
                ['status' => 1, 'expire_at' => now()->addDays(self::CART_EXPIRE_DAYS)]
            );

            $currentCount = $cart->validItems()->count();
            if ($currentCount >= self::CART_MAX_ITEMS) {
                throw new \App\Exceptions\CartException('CART_FULL', '购物车已满，请先结算或删除商品');
            }

            // 使用 PricingService 计算单价（支持数量阶梯折扣）
            $unitPrice = $this->pricingService->calculateUnitPrice(
                $product, $paramSnapshot, $quantity, $isUrgent
            );

            $existing = $cart->validItems()
                ->where('product_id', $product->id)
                ->where('cp_summary', $cpSummary)
                ->first();

            if ($existing) {
                $newQty = $existing->quantity + $quantity;
                $newUnitPrice = $this->pricingService->calculateUnitPrice(
                    $product, $paramSnapshot, $newQty, $isUrgent
                );
                $existing->quantity = $newQty;
                $existing->unit_price = $newUnitPrice;
                $existing->total_price = $newUnitPrice * $newQty;
                $existing->param_snapshot = $paramSnapshot;
                $existing->is_urgent = $isUrgent;
                $existing->save();
                $this->refreshCartCache($cart);
                return $existing;
            }

            $item = $cart->items()->create([
                'product_id' => $product->id,
                'category_id' => $product->category_id,
                'cp_summary' => $cpSummary,
                'param_snapshot' => $paramSnapshot,
                'quantity' => $quantity,
                'unit_price' => $unitPrice,
                'total_price' => $unitPrice * $quantity,
                'file_ids' => $fileIds ?? [],
                'brand_id' => $brandId,
                'is_selected' => true,
                'is_urgent' => $isUrgent,
                'status' => 1,
                'expire_at' => now()->addDays(self::CART_EXPIRE_DAYS),
            ]);

            $this->refreshCartCache($cart);
            return $item;
        });
    }

    /**
     * 获取购物车列表
     * FR-CART-003, FR-CART-005, FR-CART-007
     *
     * FIX-P0-4: 增加优惠券计算
     */
    public function list(int $customerId, ?string $couponCode = null): array
    {
        $items = CartItem::whereHas('cart', fn ($q) => $q->where('customer_id', $customerId))
            ->with('product')
            ->orderBy('created_at', 'desc')
            ->get();

        $validItems = $items->where('status', 1);
        $selectedItems = $validItems->where('is_selected', true);

        $totalAmount = $validItems->sum('total_price');
        $selectedAmount = $selectedItems->sum('total_price');

        // 优惠券计算（仅针对选中项）
        $discountAmount = 0;
        $appliedCoupon = null;
        if ($couponCode && $selectedAmount > 0) {
            $couponResult = \App\Services\CouponService::calculateDiscount(
                customerId: $customerId,
                couponCode: $couponCode,
                items: $selectedItems,
                totalAmount: $selectedAmount
            );
            $discountAmount = $couponResult['discount_amount'] ?? 0;
            $appliedCoupon = $couponResult['coupon'] ?? null;
        }

        return [
            'items' => $items,
            'total_amount' => $totalAmount,
            'selected_amount' => $selectedAmount,
            'selected_count' => $selectedItems->sum('quantity'),
            'total_count' => $validItems->sum('quantity'),
            'invalid_count' => $items->where('status', 0)->count(),
            // 新增优惠券字段（FIX-P0-4）
            'coupon_code' => $appliedCoupon?->coupon_code ?? $couponCode,
            'coupon_id' => $appliedCoupon?->id ?? null,
            'discount_amount' => $discountAmount,
            'payable_amount' => max(0, $selectedAmount - $discountAmount),
        ];
    }

    /**
     * 更新购物车项数量（重新计价）
     * FR-CART-004
     */
    public function updateQuantity(int $customerId, int $cartItemId, int $quantity): CartItem
    {
        $item = CartItem::whereHas('cart', fn ($q) => $q->where('customer_id', $customerId))
            ->where('id', $cartItemId)
            ->firstOrFail();

        if ($quantity <= 0) {
            $item->delete();
            $this->refreshCartCache($item->cart);
            return $item;
        }

        $maxQty = $this->pricingService->getMaxQuantity($item->product_id);
        if ($quantity > $maxQty) {
            throw new \InvalidArgumentException("超出最大可购买数量: {$maxQty}");
        }

        // 重新计价：数量变化可能触发阶梯折扣
        $currentPrice = $this->pricingService->calculateUnitPrice(
            $item->product, $item->param_snapshot, $quantity, $item->is_urgent
        );

        $item->quantity = $quantity;
        $item->unit_price = $currentPrice;
        $item->total_price = $currentPrice * $quantity;
        $item->save();

        $this->refreshCartCache($item->cart);
        return $item;
    }

    /**
     * 删除购物车项
     * FR-CART-006
     */
    public function delete(int $customerId, array $cartItemIds): int
    {
        $deleted = CartItem::whereHas('cart', fn ($q) => $q->where('customer_id', $customerId))
            ->whereIn('id', $cartItemIds)
            ->delete();

        // 清理已无子项的废弃购物车
        Cart::whereDoesntHave('items')->delete();

        return $deleted;
    }

    /**
     * 切换选中状态（单选/全选）
     * FR-CART-005
     */
    public function toggleSelection(int $customerId, ?int $cartItemId, bool $isSelected): void
    {
        $query = CartItem::whereHas('cart', fn ($q) => $q->where('customer_id', $customerId));

        if ($cartItemId !== null) {
            $query->where('id', $cartItemId);
        }

        $query->update(['is_selected' => $isSelected]);
    }

    /**
     * 清空购物车
     */
    public function clear(int $customerId): int
    {
        $cart = Cart::byCustomer($customerId)->first();
        if (! $cart) {
            return 0;
        }

        return $cart->items()->delete();
    }

    /**
     * 获取选中项用于结算
     * FR-CART-008
     */
    public function getSelectedItems(int $customerId): Collection
    {
        return CartItem::whereHas('cart', fn ($q) => $q->where('customer_id', $customerId))
            ->where('is_selected', true)
            ->where('status', 1)
            ->with('product')
            ->get();
    }

    private function refreshCartCache(Cart $cart): void
    {
        $summary = [
            'total_count' => $cart->validItems()->count(),
            'selected_count' => $cart->selectedItems()->sum('quantity'),
            'selected_total' => $cart->selectedItems()->sum('total_price'),
            'invalid_count' => $cart->items()->where('status', 0)->count(),
            'updated_at' => now()->toDateTimeString(),
        ];

        if ($cart->customer_id) {
            // 购物车摘要缓存：TTL=10min，配合 Cache Tags 批量失效
            Cache::tags(['cart', "cart:{$cart->customer_id}"])
                ->put("cart:summary:{$cart->customer_id}", $summary, now()->addMinutes(10));
        }
    }
}
```

<?php

// app/Actions/Cart/AddToCartAction.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\Cart;

use App\Models\Cart;
use App\Services\CartService;

class AddToCartAction
{
    public function __construct(private CartService $cartService) {}

    public function execute(int $customerId, array $data): CartItem
    {
        return $this->cartService->add(
            customerId: $customerId,
            productId: $data['product_id'],
            cpSummary: $data['cp_summary'],
            paramSnapshot: $data['param_snapshot'],
            quantity: $data['quantity'],
            fileIds: $data['file_ids'] ?? null,
            brandId: $data['brand_id'] ?? null,
            isUrgent: $data['is_urgent'] ?? false,
        );
    }
}

```php
<?php

// app/Actions/Cart/MergeCartAction.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\Cart;

use App\Models\Cart;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Log;

class MergeCartAction
{
    public function execute(int $customerId, string $sessionId): void
    {
        $guestCart = Cart::bySession($sessionId)->with('items')->first();
        if (! $guestCart || $guestCart->items->isEmpty()) {
            return;
        }

        DB::transaction(function () use ($customerId, $guestCart) {
            $customerCart = Cart::firstOrCreate(
                ['customer_id' => $customerId],
                ['status' => 1, 'expire_at' => now()->addDays(30)]
            );

            foreach ($guestCart->items as $guestItem) {
                $existing = $customerCart->validItems()
                    ->where('product_id', $guestItem->product_id)
                    ->where('cp_summary', $guestItem->cp_summary)
                    ->first();

                if ($existing) {
                    $existing->update([
                        'quantity' => $existing->quantity + $guestItem->quantity,
                        'total_price' => $existing->unit_price * ($existing->quantity + $guestItem->quantity),
                    ]);
                } else {
                    $customerCart->items()->create($guestItem->toArray());
                }
            }

            $guestCart->items()->delete();
            $guestCart->delete();

            Log::info('[CartMerge] 购物车合并完成', [
                'customer_id' => $customerId,
                'merged_items' => $guestCart->items->count(),
            ]);
        });
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

// app/Actions/Cart/ClearExpiredCartAction.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\Cart;

use App\Models\Cart;
use App\Models\CartItem;

class ClearExpiredCartAction
{
    public function execute(): int
    {
        $deletedItems = CartItem::where('expire_at', '<', now())->delete();

        // 清理已无子项的废弃购物车
        Cart::whereDoesntHave('items')->delete();

        return $deletedItems;
    }
}

### 1.5 FormRequest 设计

```php
<?php

// app/Http/Requests/Cart/AddToCartRequest.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Requests\Cart;

use Illuminate\Foundation\Http\FormRequest;

class AddToCartRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool
    {
        return auth('sanctum')->check();
    }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'product_id'     => ['required', 'integer', 'exists:products,id'],
            'param_snapshot'  => ['required', 'array'],
            'quantity'       => ['required', 'integer', 'min:1', 'max:99999'],
        ];
    }
}
```

    }

    {

            'quantity'     => ['required', 'integer', 'min:0'],

### 1.6 Resource 设计

```php
<?php

// app/Http/Resources/CartItemResource.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Resources;

use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\JsonResource;

class CartItemResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'id'             => $this->id,
            'product_id'     => $this->product_id,
            'product_name'   => $this->product?->name,
            'thumbnail'      => $this->product?->thumbnail,
            'cp_summary'     => $this->cp_summary,
            'param_snapshot' => $this->param_snapshot,
            'spec_summary'   => \App\Services\CpSummaryParser::toHumanReadable($this->cp_summary),
            'quantity'       => $this->quantity,
            'unit_price'     => $this->unit_price,     // 单位：分，前端需自行 /100
            'total_price'    => $this->total_price,    // 单位：分
            'is_selected'    => $this->is_selected,
            'is_urgent'      => $this->is_urgent,
            'status'         => $this->status,         // 1=有效 0=失效
            'invalid_reason' => $this->status === 0 ? $this->remark : null,
            'file_ids'       => $this->file_ids,
            'created_at'     => $this->created_at?->toDateTimeString(),
        ];
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

// app/Http/Resources/CartListResource.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Resources;

use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\JsonResource;

class CartListResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'items'           => CartItemResource::collection($this['items']),
            'total_amount'    => $this['total_amount'],
            'selected_amount' => $this['selected_amount'],
            'selected_count'  => $this['selected_count'],
            'total_count'     => $this['total_count'],
            'invalid_count'   => $this['invalid_count'] ?? 0,
            // 新增优惠券字段（FIX-P0-4）
            'coupon_code'     => $this['coupon_code'] ?? null,
            'coupon_id'       => $this['coupon_id'] ?? null,
            'discount_amount' => $this['discount_amount'] ?? 0,
            'payable_amount'  => $this['payable_amount'] ?? $this['selected_amount'],
        ];
    }
}
```

### 1.7 Controller 设计

```php
<?php

// app/Http/Controllers/Api/CartController.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Controllers\Api;

use App\Actions\Cart\AddToCartAction;
use App\Actions\Cart\ClearCartAction;
use App\Actions\Cart\DeleteCartItemsAction;
use App\Actions\Cart\GetCartListAction;
use App\Actions\Cart\GetSelectedCartItemsAction;
use App\Actions\Cart\ToggleCartSelectionAction;
use App\Actions\Cart\UpdateCartItemAction;
use App\Http\Controllers\Controller;
use App\Http\Requests\Cart\AddToCartRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Cart\DeleteCartItemsRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Cart\ToggleSelectionRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Cart\UpdateCartItemRequest;
use App\Http\Resources\CartItemResource;
use App\Http\Resources\CartListResource;
use Illuminate\Http\JsonResponse;

/**
 * 购物车模块API控制器
 * 覆盖PRD: FR-CART-001 ~ FR-CART-009
 */
class CartController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        private AddToCartAction $addToCart,
        private GetCartListAction $getCartList,
        private UpdateCartItemAction $updateCartItem,
        private DeleteCartItemsAction $deleteCartItems,
        private ToggleCartSelectionAction $toggleSelection,
        private ClearCartAction $clearCart,
        private GetSelectedCartItemsAction $getSelectedItems,
        private CheckCartValidityAction $checkCartValidity,
        private MergeCartAction $mergeCart,              // 新增（FIX-P0-3）
        private ClearExpiredCartAction $clearExpiredCart, // 新增（FIX-P0-3）
    ) {}

    /**
     * 加入购物车
     * FR-CART-001, FR-CART-002
     * POST /api/Cart/Add
     */
    public function add(AddToCartRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $cartItem = $this->addToCart->execute(
            customerId: auth('sanctum')->id(),
            data: $request->validated(),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'cart_item_id' => $cartItem->id,
            'message' => '已加入购物车',
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 购物车列表
     * FR-CART-003, FR-CART-005, FR-CART-007
     * GET /api/Cart/List
     *
     * FIX-P0-4: 支持优惠券传参
     */
    public function list(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $data = $this->getCartList->execute(
            customerId: auth('sanctum')->id(),
            couponCode: $request->input('coupon_code'),
        );
        return $this->success(new CartListResource($data));
    }

    /**
     * 修改数量
     * FR-CART-004
     * POST /api/Cart/Update
     */
    public function update(UpdateCartItemRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $item = $this->updateCartItem->execute(
            customerId: auth('sanctum')->id(),
            cartItemId: $request->input('cart_item_id'),
            quantity: $request->input('quantity'),
        );

        return $this->success([
            'cart_item_id' => $item->id,
            'quantity'     => $item->quantity,
            'total_price'  => $item->total_price,
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 删除商品（支持批量）
     * FR-CART-006
     * POST /api/Cart/Delete
     */
    public function delete(DeleteCartItemsRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $count = $this->deleteCartItems->execute(
            customerId: auth('sanctum')->id(),
            cartItemIds: $request->input('cart_item_ids'),
        );

        return $this->success(['deleted_count' => $count]);
    }

    /**
     * 切换选中状态（单选/全选）
     * FR-CART-005
     * POST /api/Cart/ToggleSelection
     */
    public function toggleSelection(ToggleSelectionRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->toggleSelection->execute(
            customerId: auth('sanctum')->id(),
            cartItemId: $request->input('cart_item_id'),
            isSelected: $request->boolean('is_selected'),
        );

        return $this->success(['message' => '选中状态已更新']);
    }

    /**
     * 清空购物车
     * POST /api/Cart/Clear
     */
    public function clear(): JsonResponse
    {
        $count = $this->clearCart->execute(auth('sanctum')->id());
        return $this->success(['cleared_count' => $count]);
    }

    /**
     * 获取选中项（用于结算跳转）
     * FR-CART-008
     * GET /api/Cart/SelectedItems
     */
    public function selectedItems(): JsonResponse
    {
        $items = $this->getSelectedItems->execute(auth('sanctum')->id());
        return $this->success(CartItemResource::collection($items));
    }

    /**
     * 购物车结算前置校验
     * FR-CART-008
     * POST /api/Cart/Checkout
     *
     * 在跳转订单确认页前执行全量校验：
     * 1. 失效检测（商品下架/参数变更/价格变动>10%）
     * 2. 库存校验
     * 3. 重新计算选中项最新价格
     * 4. 返回订单确认页所需数据
     */
    public function checkout(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $customerId = auth('sanctum')->id();
        $couponCode = $request->input('coupon_code');

        // Step 1: 全量失效检测
        $invalidCount = $this->checkCartValidity->execute($customerId);

        // Step 2: 获取当前有效选中项
        $items = $this->getSelectedItems->execute($customerId);

        if ($items->isEmpty()) {
            return $this->error('没有选中的商品或可结算的商品已失效', 422);
        }

        // Step 3: 库存校验（注入 InventoryService，替代反射）
        foreach ($items as $item) {
            $stockOk = \App\Services\Inventory\InventoryService::checkStock(
                $item->product_id,
                $item->quantity
            );
            if (! $stockOk) {
                return $this->error(
                    sprintf('商品 "%s" 库存不足，当前可购买数量不足', $item->product?->name ?? '未知商品'),
                    422
                );
            }
        }

        // Step 4: 重新计算最新价格并汇总
        $selectedAmount = 0;
        $updatedItems = [];
        foreach ($items as $item) {
            $currentPrice = \App\Facades\Pricing::quickEstimate(
                $item->product_id,
                $item->cp_summary,
                $item->quantity
            );
            $subtotal = $currentPrice * $item->quantity;
            $selectedAmount += $subtotal;

            $updatedItems[] = [
                'cart_item_id' => $item->id,
                'product_id'   => $item->product_id,
                'product_name' => $item->product?->name,
                'thumbnail'    => $item->product?->thumbnail,
                'cp_summary'   => $item->cp_summary,
                'quantity'     => $item->quantity,
                'unit_price'   => $currentPrice,
                'subtotal'     => $subtotal,
            ];
        }

        // Step 5: 优惠券校验与锁定（结算阶段锁定，防止超用）
        $discountAmount = 0;
        $couponInfo = null;
        if ($couponCode) {
            $couponResult = \App\Services\CouponService::validateAndLock(
                customerId: $customerId,
                couponCode: $couponCode,
                totalAmount: $selectedAmount,
                items: $items,
            );
            if (! $couponResult['valid']) {
                return $this->error($couponResult['message'] ?? '优惠券无效或不符合使用条件', 422);
            }
            $discountAmount = $couponResult['discount_amount'];
            $couponInfo = $couponResult['coupon'];
        }

        // Step 6: 返回订单确认页数据
        return $this->success([
            'items'           => $updatedItems,
            'total_quantity'  => $items->sum('quantity'),
            'selected_amount' => $selectedAmount,
            'discount_amount' => $discountAmount,
            'payable_amount'  => max(0, $selectedAmount - $discountAmount),
            'coupon_code'     => $couponInfo?->coupon_code ?? $couponCode,
            'coupon_id'       => $couponInfo?->id ?? null,
            'invalid_count'   => $invalidCount,
            'invalid_items'   => $this->getInvalidItems($customerId),
            'redirect_to'     => '/stock/submit',
            'message'         => $invalidCount > 0
                ? sprintf('结算准备完成，已标记 %d 个失效商品', $invalidCount)
                : '结算校验通过',
        ]);
    }

    /**
     * 获取失效商品明细（辅助方法）
     */
    private function getInvalidItems(int $customerId): array
    {
        return CartItem::whereHas('cart', fn ($q) => $q->where('customer_id', $customerId))
            ->where('status', 0)
            ->with('product')
            ->get()
            ->map(fn ($item) => [
                'cart_item_id' => $item->id,
                'product_name' => $item->product?->name ?? '未知商品',
                'reason'       => $item->remark,
            ])
            ->toArray();
    }

    /**
     * 登录后合并访客购物车
     * POST /api/Cart/Merge
     */
    public function merge(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $sessionId = $request->input('session_id');
        if (empty($sessionId)) {
            return $this->error('缺少会话标识', 422);
        }

        $this->mergeCart->execute(
            customerId: auth('sanctum')->id(),
            sessionId: $sessionId,
        );

        return $this->success(['message' => '购物车合并完成']);
    }

    /**
     * 清理过期购物车项（管理员或系统调用）
     * POST /api/Cart/ClearExpired
     */
    public function clearExpired(): JsonResponse
    {
        $count = $this->clearExpiredCart->execute();
        return $this->success(['cleared_count' => $count]);
    }
}
```

---

### 1.8 路由设计

```php
<?php

use App\Http\Controllers\Api\CartController;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Route;

Route::prefix('Cart')->middleware(['auth:sanctum', 'throttle:api'])->group(function () {
    // 用户级接口（补充文档已有）
    Route::post('Add', [CartController::class, 'add']);
    Route::get('List', [CartController::class, 'list']);              // ✅ GET，符合RESTful
    Route::post('Update', [CartController::class, 'update']);
    Route::post('Delete', [CartController::class, 'delete']);         // ✅ Delete语义更准确
    Route::post('ToggleSelection', [CartController::class, 'toggleSelection']);
    Route::post('Clear', [CartController::class, 'clear']);
    Route::get('SelectedItems', [CartController::class, 'selectedItems']);
    Route::post('Checkout', [CartController::class, 'checkout']);     // 结算前置校验

    // 系统/登录级接口（原始SDD有，补充文档缺失，需补回）
    Route::post('Merge', [CartController::class, 'merge']);            // 登录后合并访客购物车
    Route::post('ClearExpired', [CartController::class, 'clearExpired']); // 管理员/系统清理过期项
});
```

---

### 1.9 FR-CART 映射汇总

| FR编号 | PRD功能描述 | Controller::Action | API路由 | 关联Action/Service |
|--------|------------|-------------------|---------|-------------------|
| FR-CART-001 | 商品详情页支持"加入购物车" | `CartController::add` | `POST /api/Cart/Add` | `AddToCartAction` / `CartService::add()` |
| FR-CART-002 | 同一商品不同规格视为不同购物车项 | `CartController::add` | `POST /api/Cart/Add` | `CartService::generateSpecHash()` 唯一索引 |
| FR-CART-003 | 购物车列表展示 | `CartController::list` | `GET /api/Cart/List` | `GetCartListAction` / `CartService::list()` |
| FR-CART-004 | 支持修改数量 | `CartController::update` | `POST /api/Cart/Update` | `UpdateCartItemAction` / `CartService::updateQuantity()` |
| FR-CART-005 | 支持单选/全选 | `CartController::toggleSelection` | `POST /api/Cart/ToggleSelection` | `ToggleCartSelectionAction` |
| FR-CART-006 | 支持删除商品 | `CartController::delete` | `POST /api/Cart/Delete` | `DeleteCartItemsAction` |
| FR-CART-007 | 底部显示合计金额、结算按钮 | `CartController::list` | `GET /api/Cart/List` | 列表返回 `total_amount` / `selected_amount` |
| FR-CART-008 | 选中商品点击"结算"跳转订单确认页 | `CartController::selectedItems` → `OrderController::create` | `GET /api/Cart/SelectedItems` | `GetSelectedCartItemsAction` |
| FR-CART-009 | 路由：`/stock/cart` → `/stock/submit` | 前端路由配置 | Vue Router | 前端 `/stock/cart` 页面结算后跳转 `/stock/submit` |

---

## 2. 模块五：订单系统（FR-ORDER-021~058）

> **审查结论**：FR-ORDER-021~058 大量缺失。本节聚焦三类重点：
> 1. **状态流转**（FR-ORDER-021~030）：取消/删除/复制、审核不通过/待修改/已修改流转
> 2. **定金与修改**（FR-ORDER-031~040）：退款子状态机、多级定金阶段、修改确认
> 3. **订单元数据**（FR-ORDER-051~058）：来源(source)、Sign位掩码、配送方式、发票

---

### 2.1 状态机补充设计

#### 2.1.1 OrderStatus 扩展（新增子状态概念）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 订单主状态枚举
 * PRD键名: orders.status
 */
enum OrderStatus: int
{
    case CANCELLED          = 0;    // 已取消
    case REGISTERED         = 1;    // 已登记（客户侧展示为"待付款"）
    case REVOKED_AUDIT      = 2;    // 已撤审
    case AUDITED            = 3;    // 已审核
    case ORDERED            = 11;   // 已下单
    case REVOKED_ORDERED    = 12;   // 已撤审下单
    case AUDITED_ORDERED    = 13;   // 已审核下单
    case ASSIGNED           = 15;   // 已分配
    case WORK_ORDERED       = 17;   // 已开工单
    case OUTSOURCED         = 20;   // 已外协
    case SCAN_RETURNED      = 54;   // 扫描返厂
    case RETURNED           = 55;   // 已返厂
    case REVOKED_INBOUND    = 60;   // 已撤销入库
    case PARTIAL_INBOUND    = 61;   // 部分已入库
    case INBOUND            = 62;   // 已入库（客户侧展示为"待发货"）
    case PRE_OUTBOUND       = 65;   // 预处理出库
    case OUTBOUND           = 66;   // 已出库（客户侧展示为"已发货"）
    case NORMAL_OUTBOUND    = 67;   // 正常出库
    case COMPLETED          = 69;   // 已完成
    case PENDING_CONTACT    = 100;  // 待沟通
    case FILE_NOT_UPLOADED  = 101;  // 未上传/文件审核不通过（客户侧展示为"待修改"）
    case EXCEPTION          = 255;  // 异常

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::CANCELLED         => '已取消',
            self::REGISTERED        => '已登记',
            self::REVOKED_AUDIT     => '已撤审',
            self::AUDITED           => '已审核',
            self::ORDERED           => '已下单',
            self::REVOKED_ORDERED   => '已撤审下单',
            self::AUDITED_ORDERED   => '已审核下单',
            self::ASSIGNED          => '已分配',
            self::WORK_ORDERED      => '已开工单',
            self::OUTSOURCED        => '已外协',
            self::SCAN_RETURNED     => '扫描返厂',
            self::RETURNED          => '已返厂',
            self::REVOKED_INBOUND   => '已撤销入库',
            self::PARTIAL_INBOUND   => '部分已入库',
            self::INBOUND           => '已入库',
            self::PRE_OUTBOUND      => '预处理出库',
            self::OUTBOUND          => '已出库',
            self::NORMAL_OUTBOUND   => '正常出库',
            self::COMPLETED         => '已完成',
            self::PENDING_CONTACT   => '待沟通',
            self::FILE_NOT_UPLOADED => '文件审核不通过',
            self::EXCEPTION         => '异常',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否允许流转到目标状态
     * 核心状态机校验规则
     */
    public function canTransitionTo(self $target): bool
    {
        return match ([$this, $target]) {
            // 登记 → 审核/取消
            [self::REGISTERED, self::AUDITED],
            [self::REGISTERED, self::CANCELLED] => true,
            // 审核 → 下单/取消
            [self::AUDITED, self::ORDERED],
            [self::AUDITED, self::CANCELLED] => true,
            // 下单 → 分配
            [self::ORDERED, self::ASSIGNED],
            [self::REVOKED_ORDERED, self::ASSIGNED],
            [self::AUDITED_ORDERED, self::ASSIGNED] => true,
            // 分配 → 开工单
            [self::ASSIGNED, self::WORK_ORDERED] => true,
            // 开工单 → 外协/入库
            [self::WORK_ORDERED, self::OUTSOURCED],
            [self::WORK_ORDERED, self::INBOUND] => true,
            // 外协 → 入库/返厂
            [self::OUTSOURCED, self::INBOUND],
            [self::OUTSOURCED, self::SCAN_RETURNED] => true,
            // 扫描返厂 → 返厂
            [self::SCAN_RETURNED, self::RETURNED] => true,
            // 返厂 → 入库/撤销入库
            [self::RETURNED, self::INBOUND],
            [self::RETURNED, self::REVOKED_INBOUND] => true,
            // 撤销入库 → 部分入库/入库
            [self::REVOKED_INBOUND, self::PARTIAL_INBOUND],
            [self::REVOKED_INBOUND, self::INBOUND] => true,
            // 部分入库 → 入库
            [self::PARTIAL_INBOUND, self::INBOUND] => true,
            // 入库 → 出库/预处理出库
            [self::INBOUND, self::OUTBOUND],
            [self::INBOUND, self::NORMAL_OUTBOUND],
            [self::INBOUND, self::PRE_OUTBOUND] => true,
            // 预处理出库 → 出库
            [self::PRE_OUTBOUND, self::OUTBOUND],
            [self::PRE_OUTBOUND, self::NORMAL_OUTBOUND] => true,
            // 出库 → 完成
            [self::OUTBOUND, self::COMPLETED],
            [self::NORMAL_OUTBOUND, self::COMPLETED] => true,
            // 文件审核不通过 → 重新登记
            [self::FILE_NOT_UPLOADED, self::REGISTERED] => true,
            default => false,
        };
    }

    /**
     * FM → nM 客户展示状态映射
     * PRD 9.3 节双状态映射规则
     */
    public function toCustomerStatus(?OrderModifyStatus $modifyStatus = null): CustomerOrderStatus
    {
        // modifyStatus 处于修改流程中（非默认/未修改/已确认），统一展示为"待修改"
        if ($modifyStatus !== null && $modifyStatus->isInModifyProcess()) {
            return CustomerOrderStatus::PENDING_MODIFY;
        }

        return match ($this) {
            self::CANCELLED,
            self::EXCEPTION => CustomerOrderStatus::CANCELLED,

            self::REGISTERED => CustomerOrderStatus::PENDING_PAYMENT,

            // nM=6 待生产：早期生产环节（审核后 ~ 开工单前）
            self::AUDITED, self::ORDERED, self::REVOKED_ORDERED,
            self::AUDITED_ORDERED, self::ASSIGNED => CustomerOrderStatus::PENDING_PRODUCTION,

            // nM=3 生产中：实际生产环节（开工单后 ~ 入库前）
            self::WORK_ORDERED, self::OUTSOURCED, self::SCAN_RETURNED,
            self::RETURNED, self::REVOKED_INBOUND, self::PARTIAL_INBOUND => CustomerOrderStatus::IN_PRODUCTION,

            // 已入库 → 待发货
            self::INBOUND, self::PRE_OUTBOUND => CustomerOrderStatus::PENDING_SHIP,

            // 已出库 → 已发货/配送中
            self::OUTBOUND, self::NORMAL_OUTBOUND => CustomerOrderStatus::SHIPPED,

            // 已完成
            self::COMPLETED => CustomerOrderStatus::COMPLETED,

            // 特殊状态
            self::PENDING_CONTACT,
            self::FILE_NOT_UPLOADED => CustomerOrderStatus::PENDING_MODIFY,

            default => CustomerOrderStatus::IN_PRODUCTION,
        };
    }

    /**
     * 是否为"待生产"阶段（nM=6 映射用）
     */
    public function isPendingProduction(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [
            self::AUDITED,
            self::ORDERED,
            self::REVOKED_ORDERED,
            self::AUDITED_ORDERED,
            self::ASSIGNED,
        ], true);
    }

    /**
     * 是否已进入生产流程（不可取消/不可直接退款需走售后）
     */
    public function isInProduction(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [
            self::AUDITED,
            self::ORDERED,
            self::REVOKED_ORDERED,
            self::AUDITED_ORDERED,
            self::ASSIGNED,
            self::WORK_ORDERED,
            self::OUTSOURCED,
            self::SCAN_RETURNED,
            self::RETURNED,
            self::REVOKED_INBOUND,
            self::PARTIAL_INBOUND,
            self::INBOUND,
        ], true);
    }
}
```

#### 2.1.2 ModifyStatus 枚举（修改状态子状态机）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 订单修改状态子状态机
 * PRD键名: orders.modify_status
 * FR-ORDER-040 ~ FR-ORDER-043
 */
enum ModifyStatus: int
{
    case NONE        = 0; // 无修改
    case APPLYING    = 1; // 客户申请修改中（FR-ORDER-024）
    case MODIFIED    = 2; // 客户已修改/已标记（FR-ORDER-025, FR-ORDER-041）
    case CONFIRMED   = 3; // 客户确认修改结果（FR-ORDER-042）
    case REJECTED    = 4; // 平台拒绝修改

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::NONE     => '无修改',
            self::APPLYING => '修改申请中',
            self::MODIFIED => '已修改待确认',
            self::CONFIRMED => '修改已确认',
            self::REJECTED  => '修改已拒绝',
        };
    }

    public function canTransitionTo(self $target): bool
    {
        return match ([$this, $target]) {
            [self::NONE, self::APPLYING]    => true,
            [self::APPLYING, self::MODIFIED] => true,
            [self::MODIFIED, self::CONFIRMED] => true,
            [self::MODIFIED, self::REJECTED]  => true,
            [self::APPLYING, self::REJECTED]  => true,
            [self::REJECTED, self::NONE]      => true,
            [self::CONFIRMED, self::NONE]     => true,
            default => false,
        };
    }
}
```

#### 2.1.3 RefundStatus 枚举（退款子状态机）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 退款子状态枚举
 * PRD键名: orders.refund_status
 * FR-ORDER-031 ~ FR-ORDER-034
 */
enum RefundStatus: int
{
    case NONE          = 0; // 无退款
    case APPLYING      = 1; // 退款申请中
    case AUDITING      = 2; // 后台审核中
    case REFUNDED      = 3; // 已退款（FR-ORDER-032）
    case REJECTED      = 4; // 退款被拒绝（FR-ORDER-033）

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::NONE     => '无退款',
            self::APPLYING => '退款申请中',
            self::AUDITING => '审核中',
            self::REFUNDED => '已退款',
            self::REJECTED => '退款已拒绝',
        };
    }
}
```

#### 2.1.4 DepositPhase 枚举（多级定金阶段）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 定金阶段枚举
 * PRD键名: orders.deposit_phase / unPaidDeposit
 * FR-ORDER-035 ~ FR-ORDER-038, FR-PAY-029
 */
enum DepositPhase: int
{
    case PHASE_0 = 0; // unPaidDeposit0: 下单待确认，未付任何款项
    case PHASE_1 = 1; // unPaidDeposit1: 审核通过待付定金
    case PHASE_2 = 2; // unPaidDeposit2: 生产中待付尾款
    case PHASE_6 = 6; // unPaidDeposit6: 大客户特殊定金
    case PHASE_7 = 7; // unPaidDeposit7: 账期订单到期结算

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::PHASE_0 => '待确认（未付款）',
            self::PHASE_1 => '待付定金',
            self::PHASE_2 => '待付尾款',
            self::PHASE_6 => '特殊定金',
            self::PHASE_7 => '账期结算',
        };
    }

    /**
     * 当前阶段是否允许支付
     */
    public function isPayable(): bool
    {
        return in_array($this, [self::PHASE_0, self::PHASE_1, self::PHASE_2, self::PHASE_6, self::PHASE_7], true);
    }

    /**
     * 下一阶段
     */
    public function next(): ?self
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::PHASE_0 => self::PHASE_1,
            self::PHASE_1 => self::PHASE_2,
            self::PHASE_2 => null, // 尾款付完即完成
            self::PHASE_6 => null,
            self::PHASE_7 => null,
        };
    }
}
```

#### 2.1.5 OrderSource 枚举（订单来源）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**

 * PRD键名: orders.source (WM)

enum OrderSource: int
{
    case OFFICIAL_WEBSITE = 0; // 官网
    case MINI_PROGRAM   = 1; // 小程序
    case QUOTE_WEBSITE  = 2; // 报价网站
    case AGENT          = 3; // 代下单
    case LOCAL          = 4; // 本地订单导入

    public function label(): string
    {
        return match ($this) {
            self::OFFICIAL_WEBSITE => '官网',
            self::MINI_PROGRAM   => '小程序',
            self::QUOTE_WEBSITE  => '报价网站',
            self::AGENT          => '代下单',
            self::LOCAL          => '本地订单',
        };
