#### 2.1.6 OrderSign 位掩码枚举（Sign位定义）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Enums;

/**
 * 订单Sign位掩码枚举
 * PRD键名: orders.order_sign (LM位掩码)
 * FR-ORDER-058-A
 */
enum OrderSign: int
{
    case IS_URGENT        = 1 << 0;  // 0x1: 加急订单
    /** @deprecated FIX-P0: 样品订单使用独立sample_orders表，不再通过IS_SAMPLE标志区分 */
    case IS_SAMPLE        = 1 << 1;  // 0x2: 样品订单（已废弃）
    case IS_BATCH         = 1 << 2;  // 0x4: 批量订单
    case IS_CLOUDHOUSE    = 1 << 3;  // 0x8: 云仓订单
    case IS_LOCAL         = 1 << 4;  // 0x10: 本地订单
    case IS_AGENT         = 1 << 5;  // 0x20: 代下单
    case HAS_INVOICE      = 1 << 6;  // 0x40: 已开票
    case HAS_AFTER_SALE   = 1 << 7;  // 0x80: 有售后
    case HAS_MODIFY       = 1 << 8;  // 0x100: 有修改记录
    case MULTI_ADDRESS    = 1 << 9;  // 0x200: 多地址配送
    case PAID_DEPOSIT     = 1 << 10; // 0x400: 已付定金
    case PAID_BALANCE     = 1 << 11; // 0x800: 已付尾款

    /**
     * 检查位掩码中是否包含当前标志
     */
    public function isSet(int $signValue): bool
    {
        return ($signValue & $this->value) === $this->value;
    }

    /**
     * 设置标志位
     */
    public static function setFlag(int &$signValue, self $flag, bool $enabled = true): void
    {
        if ($enabled) {
            $signValue |= $flag->value;
        } else {
            $signValue &= ~$flag->value;
        }
    }
}
```

---

### 2.2 Service 层设计

#### 2.2.1 OrderStatusTransitionService（订单状态流转服务）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services;

use App\Enums\DepositPhase;
use App\Enums\ModifyStatus;
use App\Enums\OrderSign;
use App\Enums\OrderStatus;
use App\Enums\RefundStatus;
use App\Models\Order;
use App\Models\OrderStatusHistory;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

/**
 * 订单状态流转服务
 * FR-ORDER-021 ~ FR-ORDER-033, FR-ORDER-040 ~ FR-ORDER-043
 *
 * FIX-P0-1: 全部状态常量已按主文档完整版 OrderStatus 枚举重新映射
 * FIX-P0-3: original_status → original_status
 */
class OrderStatusTransitionService
{
    public function __construct(
        private NotificationService $notificationService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-021: 取消订单（待付款/已登记 → 已取消）
     */
    public function cancel(Order $order, ?string $reason = null): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $reason) {
            $this->assertCanCancel($order);

            $originalStatus = $order->status;
            $order->status = OrderStatus::CANCELLED;
            $order->cancel_reason = $reason;
            $order->cancelled_at = now();
            $order->save();

            $this->recordHistory($order, $originalStatus, OrderStatus::CANCELLED, '客户取消订单');
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-022: 审核不通过（生产中 → 文件未上传/审核不通过）
     *
     * FIX: PENDING_REVIEW(8) 在完整版中不存在，改为 FILE_NOT_UPLOADED(101)
     */
    public function rejectFileAudit(Order $order, string $rejectReason): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $rejectReason) {
            $order->audit_status = 3; // kM=3 审核不通过
            $order->audit_remark = $rejectReason;
            $order->status = OrderStatus::FILE_NOT_UPLOADED;
            $order->save();

            $this->notificationService->sendToCustomer(
                $order->customer_id,
                '文件审核不通过',
                "订单 {$order->order_sn} 文件审核不通过，原因：{$rejectReason}"
            );
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-023: 重新提交（审核不通过 → 已登记/重新进入审核）
     *
     * FIX: PENDING_REVIEW → FILE_NOT_UPLOADED; IN_PRODUCTION → REGISTERED
     */
    public function resubmit(Order $order): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order) {
            if ($order->audit_status !== 3) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('当前订单状态不允许重新提交');
            }

            $order->audit_status = 1; // 待审核
            $order->status = OrderStatus::REGISTERED;
            $order->resubmitted_at = now();
            $order->save();

            $this->recordHistory(
                $order,
                OrderStatus::FILE_NOT_UPLOADED,
                OrderStatus::REGISTERED,
                '客户重新提交文件'
            );
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-024 / FR-ORDER-040: 申请修改（生产中 → 待修改）
     *
     * FIX: IN_PRODUCTION 判断改为 isInProduction()；ModifyStatus → OrderModifyStatus
     */
    public function applyModify(Order $order, string $modifyContent): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $modifyContent) {
            $this->assertCanModify($order);

            $order->modify_status = OrderModifyStatus::NOT_MODIFIED->value;
            $order->modify_content = $modifyContent;
            $order->modify_applied_at = now();
            OrderSign::setFlag($order->order_sign, OrderSign::HAS_MODIFY, true);
            $order->save();

            $order->modifyHistories()->create([
                'content' => $modifyContent,
                'status'  => OrderModifyStatus::NOT_MODIFIED->value,
            ]);

            $this->recordHistory($order, $order->status, $order->status, '客户申请修改：' . $modifyContent);
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-025 / FR-ORDER-041: 客户标记已修改
     *
     * FIX: ModifyStatus → OrderModifyStatus
     */
    public function markModified(Order $order): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order) {
            if ($order->modify_status !== OrderModifyStatus::NOT_MODIFIED->value) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('当前状态不允许标记已修改');
            }

            $order->modify_status = OrderModifyStatus::MODIFIED->value;
            $order->save();

            $order->modifyHistories()->latest()->first()?->update([
                'status' => OrderModifyStatus::MODIFIED->value,
            ]);
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-042: 客户确认修改结果
     *
     * FIX: ModifyStatus → OrderModifyStatus
     */
    public function confirmModify(Order $order): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order) {
            if ($order->modify_status !== OrderModifyStatus::MODIFIED->value) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('当前状态不允许确认修改');
            }

            $order->modify_status = OrderModifyStatus::CONFIRMED->value;
            $order->modify_confirmed_at = now();
            $order->save();

            $order->modifyHistories()->latest()->first()?->update([
                'status' => OrderModifyStatus::CONFIRMED->value,
            ]);

            $this->notificationService->sendToAdmin(
                '修改待确认',
                "订单 {$order->order_sn} 客户已确认修改，请平台审核恢复生产"
            );
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-026 / FR-ORDER-043: 平台确认修改，恢复生产
     *
     * FIX: ModifyStatus → OrderModifyStatus; 主状态保持不变（修改不改变 FM）
     */
    public function platformConfirmModify(Order $order): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order) {
            if ($order->modify_status !== OrderModifyStatus::CONFIRMED->value) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('客户未确认修改，无法恢复生产');
            }

            $order->modify_status = OrderModifyStatus::DEFAULT->value;
            // 主状态在修改期间未改变，无需恢复；清除 modify_status 即可
            $order->save();

            $this->recordHistory(
                $order,
                $order->status,
                $order->status,
                '平台确认修改，恢复生产'
            );
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-027: 生产中 → 待发货（生产完成入库）
     *
     * FIX: IN_PRODUCTION → isInProduction() 判断；PENDING_DELIVERY → INBOUND(62)
     */
    public function toDelivering(Order $order): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order) {
            if (! $order->status->isInProduction()) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('订单不在生产流程中，无法流转到待发货');
            }

            $originalStatus = $order->status;
            $order->status = OrderStatus::INBOUND;
            $order->production_completed_at = now();
            $order->save();

            $this->recordHistory($order, $originalStatus, OrderStatus::INBOUND, '生产完成，已入库待发货');
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-028: 待发货 → 已发货（物流揽收，快递单号回填）
     *
     * FIX: PENDING_DELIVERY → INBOUND(62) 判断；SHIPPED → OUTBOUND(66)
     */
    public function toShipped(Order $order, string $expressNo, string $expressCompany): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $expressNo, $expressCompany) {
            if ($order->status !== OrderStatus::INBOUND) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('订单未入库，无法发货');
            }

            $originalStatus = $order->status;
            $order->status = OrderStatus::OUTBOUND;
            $order->express_no = $expressNo;
            $order->express_company = $expressCompany;
            $order->shipped_at = now();
            $order->save();

            $this->recordHistory(
                $order,
                $originalStatus,
                OrderStatus::OUTBOUND,
                "已发货：{$expressCompany} {$expressNo}"
            );
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-029: 已发货 → 已完成（客户确认收货或自动确认）
     *
     * FIX: SHIPPED → OUTBOUND(66) 判断；COMPLETED → COMPLETED(69)
     */
    public function toCompleted(Order $order, bool $autoConfirm = false): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $autoConfirm) {
            if ($order->status !== OrderStatus::OUTBOUND && $order->status !== OrderStatus::NORMAL_OUTBOUND) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('订单未发货，无法完成');
            }

            $originalStatus = $order->status;
            $order->status = OrderStatus::COMPLETED;
            $order->completed_at = now();
            $order->is_auto_confirmed = $autoConfirm;
            $order->save();

            $msg = $autoConfirm ? '7天自动确认收货' : '客户确认收货';
            $this->recordHistory($order, $originalStatus, OrderStatus::COMPLETED, $msg);
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-031: 申请退款（任意主状态 → 退款中）
     *
     * FIX: original_status → original_status
     */
    public function applyRefund(Order $order, float $amount, string $reason): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $amount, $reason) {
            if ($order->refund_status !== RefundStatus::NONE->value) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('订单已有退款进行中');
            }

            $order->original_status = $order->status->value;
            $order->refund_status = RefundStatus::APPLYING->value;
            $order->refund_amount = $amount;
            $order->refund_reason = $reason;
            $order->refund_applied_at = now();
            $order->save();

            $this->notificationService->sendToAdmin(
                '退款申请',
                "订单 {$order->order_sn} 申请退款 {$amount} 元，原因：{$reason}"
            );
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-032: 退款中 → 已退款
     *
     * FIX-P0-2: 删除错误的状态恢复逻辑（退款成功应保持终态）
     * FIX-P0-3: original_status → original_status
     */
    public function approveRefund(Order $order): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order) {
            if ($order->refund_status !== RefundStatus::APPLYING->value
                && $order->refund_status !== RefundStatus::AUDITING->value) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('订单不在退款审核状态');
            }

            $order->refund_status = RefundStatus::REFUNDED->value;
            $order->refunded_at = now();

            // ✅ FIX-P0-2: 退款成功保持终态，不恢复原始主状态
            // 若业务需要全额退款后订单关闭，可额外设置：
            // if ($order->refund_amount >= $order->total_price) {
            //     $order->status = OrderStatus::CANCELLED;
            // }

            $order->save();
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-033: 退款中 → 原状态（拒绝退款）
     *
     * FIX-P0-3: original_status → original_status
     */
    public function rejectRefund(Order $order, string $reason): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $reason) {
            if ($order->refund_status !== RefundStatus::APPLYING->value
                && $order->refund_status !== RefundStatus::AUDITING->value) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('订单不在退款审核状态');
            }

            $order->refund_status = RefundStatus::REJECTED->value;
            $order->refund_reject_reason = $reason;

            // 拒绝退款时恢复原始主状态
            if ($order->original_status !== null) {
                $order->status = OrderStatus::from($order->original_status);
            }

            $order->save();
        });
    }

    // ── 辅助方法 ──

    private function assertCanCancel(Order $order): void
    {
        $allowCancelStatuses = [
            OrderStatus::REGISTERED->value,
            OrderStatus::FILE_NOT_UPLOADED->value,
        ];

        if (! in_array($order->status->value, $allowCancelStatuses, true)) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('订单已进入生产流程，不可取消，请申请退款');
        }

        if ($order->is_paid) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('已支付订单不可直接取消，请申请退款');
        }
    }

    private function assertCanModify(Order $order): void
    {
        if (! $order->status->isInProduction()) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('仅生产中的订单可申请修改');
        }

        if ($order->modify_status !== 0
            && $order->modify_status !== OrderModifyStatus::DEFAULT->value
            && $order->modify_status !== OrderModifyStatus::CONFIRMED->value) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('订单已有修改申请进行中');
        }
    }

    private function recordHistory(Order $order, OrderStatus $from, OrderStatus $to, string $remark): void
    {
        OrderStatusHistory::create([
            'order_id'      => $order->id,
            'from_status'   => $from->value,
            'to_status'     => $to->value,
            'remark'        => $remark,
            'operator_id'   => auth('sanctum')->id(),
            'operator_type' => 'customer',
        ]);
    }
}
```

#### 2.2.2 OrderCreationService（订单创建服务，扩展source/sign/多地址）

```php
<?php

declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services;

use App\Enums\DepositPhase;
use App\Enums\OrderSign;
use App\Enums\OrderSource;
use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

/**
 * 订单创建服务（扩展字段处理）
 * FR-ORDER-050 ~ FR-ORDER-058, FR-ORDER-051-A, FR-ORDER-058-A
 */
class OrderCreationService
{
    public function __construct(
        private PricingService $pricingService,
    ) {}

    public function create(array $data): Order
    {
        return DB::transaction(function () use ($data) {
            $order = new Order();
            $order->customer_id = auth('sanctum')->id();
            $order->order_sn = $this->generateOrderSn();

            // FR-ORDER-050: 订单名称自动生成
            $order->order_name = $data['order_name'] ?? $this->generateOrderName($data);

            // FR-ORDER-051: 订单来源（source / WM）
            $order->source = ($data['source'] ?? OrderSource::OFFICIAL_WEBSITE)->value;

            // FR-ORDER-051-A: 订单创建来源（createSource / lM位掩码）
            $order->create_source = $data['create_source'] ?? 0;

            // FR-ORDER-052: 产品规格摘要（cpSummary）
            $order->cp_summary = $data['cp_summary'] ?? '';

            // FR-ORDER-056: 配送方式
            $order->delivery_type = $data['delivery_type'] ?? 1;

            // FR-ORDER-058-A: Sign位掩码初始化
            $order->order_sign = $this->buildInitialSign($data);

            // FR-ORDER-035~038, FR-PAY-029: 定金阶段
            $order->deposit_phase = ($data['deposit_phase'] ?? DepositPhase::PHASE_0)->value;
            $order->deposit_amount = $data['deposit_amount'] ?? 0;
            $order->balance_amount = $data['balance_amount'] ?? 0;

            // 价格计算
            $priceResult = $this->pricingService->calculate($data['product_id'], $data['param_snapshot'], $data['quantity']);
            $order->total_amount = $priceResult->total;
            $order->discount_amount = $priceResult->discount;
            $order->payable_amount = $priceResult->payable;

            $order->status = 1; // 待付款
            $order->save();

            return $order;
        });
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-018: 多地址配送设置
     */
    public function setMultipleDelivery(Order $order, array $addresses): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($order, $addresses) {
            if (count($addresses) > 1) {
                OrderSign::setFlag($order->order_sign, OrderSign::MULTI_ADDRESS, true);
            }

            foreach ($addresses as $idx => $addr) {
                $order->deliveryAddresses()->create([
                    'address_id'   => $addr['address_id'],
                    'quantity'     => $addr['quantity'] ?? 1,
                    'sort_order'   => $idx,
                    'contact_name' => $addr['contact_name'] ?? null,
                    'phone'        => $addr['phone'] ?? null,
                    'detail'       => $addr['detail'] ?? null,
                ]);
            }

            $order->save();
        });
    }

    private function generateOrderSn(): string
    {
        return 'YD' . date('Ymd') . strtoupper(substr(uniqid(), -6));
    }

    private function generateOrderName(array $data): string
    {
        // 如 "扬州祝宿画册骑马钉24x17CM-1万本"
        $productName = $data['product_name'] ?? '印刷品';
        $spec = $data['cp_summary'] ?? '';
        $qty = $data['quantity'] ?? 1;
        $qtyText = $qty >= 10000 ? ($qty / 10000) . '万' : $qty;
        return "{$productName}{$spec}-{$qtyText}本";
    }

    private function buildInitialSign(array $data): int
    {
        $sign = 0;
        if (!empty($data['is_urgent'])) {
            OrderSign::setFlag($sign, OrderSign::IS_URGENT, true);
        }
        if (!empty($data['is_sample'])) {
            OrderSign::setFlag($sign, OrderSign::IS_SAMPLE, true);
        }
        if (!empty($data['is_batch'])) {
            OrderSign::setFlag($sign, OrderSign::IS_BATCH, true);
        }
        return $sign;
    }
}
```

---

### 2.3 Action 层设计（新增/补全）

```php
<?php

// app/Actions/Order/CancelOrderAction.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Actions\Order;

use App\Models\Order;
use App\Services\OrderStatusTransitionService;

class CancelOrderAction
{
    public function __construct(private OrderStatusTransitionService $transitionService) {}

    public function execute(string $orderSn, ?string $reason = null): void
    {
        $order = Order::where('order_sn', $orderSn)
            ->where('customer_id', auth('sanctum')->id())
            ->firstOrFail();

        $this->transitionService->cancel($order, $reason);
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

// app/Actions/Order/ResubmitOrderAction.php

namespace App\Actions\Order;

use App\Models\Order;
use App\Services\OrderStatusTransitionService;

class ResubmitOrderAction
{
    public function __construct(private OrderStatusTransitionService $transitionService) {}

    public function execute(string $orderSn): void
    {
        $order = Order::where('order_sn', $orderSn)
            ->where('customer_id', auth('sanctum')->id())
            ->firstOrFail();

        $this->transitionService->resubmit($order);
    }
}
```

// app/Actions/Order/GetModifyHistoryAction.php

namespace App\Actions\Order;

use App\Models\Order;
use Illuminate\Support\Collection;

class GetModifyHistoryAction
{
    public function execute(string $orderSn): Collection
    {
        $order = Order::where('order_sn', $orderSn)
            ->where('customer_id', auth('sanctum')->id())
            ->firstOrFail();

        return $order->modifyHistories()->orderBy('created_at', 'desc')->get();
    }
}

### 2.4 Controller 扩展方法

以下方法需补充到 `OrderController`（已在 `supplement_api_order.md` 中定义主骨架，此处扩展缺失方法）：

```php
<?php

// 在 OrderController 中新增/补全以下方法

use App\Actions\Order\ApplyModifyAction;
use App\Actions\Order\ApplyRefundAction;
use App\Actions\Order\CancelOrderAction;
use App\Actions\Order\ConfirmModifyAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetModifyHistoryAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrderPaymentRecordsAction;
use App\Actions\Order\GetOrderRefundRecordsAction;
use App\Actions\Order\ResubmitOrderAction;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ApplyModifyRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ApplyRefundRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\CancelOrderRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ConfirmModifyRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\GetModifyHistoryRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\GetPaymentRecordsRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Order\ResubmitOrderRequest;

class OrderController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        // ... 已有依赖 ...
        private CancelOrderAction $cancelOrder,
        private ResubmitOrderAction $resubmitOrder,
        private ApplyModifyAction $applyModify,
        private ConfirmModifyAction $confirmModify,
        private ApplyRefundAction $applyRefund,
        private GetModifyHistoryAction $getModifyHistory,
        private GetOrderPaymentRecordsAction $getPaymentRecords,
        private GetOrderRefundRecordsAction $getRefundRecords,
    ) {}

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-014 / FR-ORDER-021: 取消订单
     * POST /api/Order/Cancel
     */
    public function cancel(CancelOrderRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->cancelOrder->execute(
            orderSn: $request->input('order_sn'),
            reason: $request->input('cancel_reason'),
        );

        return $this->success(['message' => '订单已取消']);
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-023: 重新提交订单（审核不通过后）
     * POST /api/Order/Resubmit
     */
    public function resubmit(ResubmitOrderRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->resubmitOrder->execute($request->input('order_sn'));
        return $this->success(['message' => '订单已重新提交']);
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-024 / FR-ORDER-040: 申请修改
     * POST /api/Order/ApplyModify
     */
    public function applyModify(ApplyModifyRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->applyModify->execute(
            orderSn: $request->input('order_sn'),
            modifyContent: $request->input('modify_content'),
        );

        return $this->success(['message' => '修改申请已提交']);
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-042: 客户确认修改结果
     * POST /api/Order/ConfirmModify
     */
    public function confirmModify(ConfirmModifyRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->confirmModify->execute($request->input('order_sn'));
        return $this->success(['message' => '修改已确认']);
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-031: 申请退款
     * POST /api/Order/ApplyRefund
     */
    public function applyRefund(ApplyRefundRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->applyRefund->execute(
            orderSn: $request->input('order_sn'),
            amount: $request->input('amount'),
            reason: $request->input('reason'),
        );

        return $this->success(['message' => '退款申请已提交']);
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-044: 获取修改历史
     * GET /api/Order/GetModifyHistory
     */
    public function modifyHistory(GetModifyHistoryRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $histories = $this->getModifyHistory->execute($request->input('order_sn'));
        return $this->success($histories);
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-017: 获取订单付款记录
     * GET /api/Order/GetOrderPaymentRecords
     */
    public function paymentRecords(GetPaymentRecordsRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $records = $this->getPaymentRecords->execute($request->input('order_sn'));
        return $this->success($records);
    }

    /**
     * FR-ORDER-018: 获取订单退款记录
     * GET /api/Order/GetOrderRefundRecordDetails
     */
    public function refundRecords(GetPaymentRecordsRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $records = $this->getRefundRecords->execute($request->input('order_sn'));
        return $this->success($records);
    }
}
```

### 2.6 FR-ORDER 映射汇总

| FR编号 | PRD功能描述 | Controller::Action | API路由 | 关联Service/枚举 |
|--------|------------|-------------------|---------|-----------------|
| FR-ORDER-021 | 待付款→已取消 | `OrderController::cancel` | `POST /api/Order/Cancel` | `OrderStatusTransitionService::cancel()` |
| FR-ORDER-022 | 生产中→审核不通过 | `AdminController::rejectFile` | `POST /api/Admin/FileAudit/Reject` | `OrderStatusTransitionService::rejectFileAudit()` |
| FR-ORDER-023 | 审核不通过→待提交 | `OrderController::resubmit` | `POST /api/Order/Resubmit` | `OrderStatusTransitionService::resubmit()` |
| FR-ORDER-024 | 生产中→待修改 | `OrderController::applyModify` | `POST /api/Order/ApplyModify` | `OrderStatusTransitionService::applyModify()` |
| FR-ORDER-025 | 待修改→已修改 | `OrderController::applyModify`（内部） | `POST /api/Order/ApplyModify` | `ModifyStatus::APPLYING→MODIFIED` |
| FR-ORDER-026 | 已修改→生产中 | `AdminController::platformConfirmModify` | `POST /api/Admin/Order/ConfirmModify` | `OrderStatusTransitionService::platformConfirmModify()` |
| FR-ORDER-027 | 生产中→待发货 | 内部/定时任务 | — | `OrderStatusTransitionService::toDelivering()` |
| FR-ORDER-028 | 待发货→已发货 | 内部/物流回调 | — | `OrderStatusTransitionService::toShipped()` |
| FR-ORDER-029 | 已发货→已完成 | `OrderController::confirmReceive` | `POST /api/Order/ConfirmReceive` | `OrderStatusTransitionService::toCompleted()` |
| FR-ORDER-030 | 已完成→售后中 | `AfterSaleController::apply` | `POST /api/AfterSale/Apply` | 售后子状态叠加 |
| FR-ORDER-031 | 任意状态→退款中 | `OrderController::applyRefund` | `POST /api/Order/ApplyRefund` | `OrderStatusTransitionService::applyRefund()` |
| FR-ORDER-032 | 退款中→已退款 | `AdminController::auditAfterSale` | `POST /api/Admin/AfterSale/Audit` | `OrderStatusTransitionService::approveRefund()` |
| FR-ORDER-033 | 退款中→原状态 | `AdminController::auditAfterSale` | `POST /api/Admin/AfterSale/Audit` | `OrderStatusTransitionService::rejectRefund()` |
| FR-ORDER-034-A | 退款路径优先级 | `RefundService::process` | 内部服务 | 原路退回→余额→提现 |
| FR-ORDER-035 | 阶段0（unPaidDeposit0） | `OrderController::create` | `POST /api/Order/Create` | `DepositPhase::PHASE_0` |
| FR-ORDER-036 | 阶段1（unPaidDeposit1） | `PayController::applyPayUrl` | `POST /api/Pay/ApplyPayUrl` | `DepositPhase::PHASE_1` |
| FR-ORDER-037 | 阶段2（unPaidDeposit2） | `PayController::applyPayUrl` | `POST /api/Pay/ApplyPayUrl` | `DepositPhase::PHASE_2` |
| FR-ORDER-038 | 阶段6（unPaidDeposit6） | `OrderController::create` | `POST /api/Order/Create` | `DepositPhase::PHASE_6` |
| FR-ORDER-039 | 阶段7（unPaidDeposit7） | `OrderController::create` | `POST /api/Order/Create` | `DepositPhase::PHASE_7` |
| FR-ORDER-040 | 生产过程中可申请修改 | `OrderController::applyModify` | `POST /api/Order/ApplyModify` | `ModifyStatus::APPLYING` |
| FR-ORDER-041 | 客户标记已修改 | `OrderController::applyModify` | `POST /api/Order/ApplyModify` | `ModifyStatus::MODIFIED` |
| FR-ORDER-042 | 客户确认修改结果 | `OrderController::confirmModify` | `POST /api/Order/ConfirmModify` | `ModifyStatus::CONFIRMED` |
| FR-ORDER-043 | 修改状态与订单状态联动 | `OrderStatusTransitionService` | 内部服务 | 修改期间锁定主状态 |
| FR-ORDER-044 | 修改历史记录 | `OrderController::modifyHistory` | `GET /api/Order/GetModifyHistory` | `Order::modifyHistories()` |
| FR-ORDER-051 | 订单来源（source） | `OrderController::create` | `POST /api/Order/Create` | `OrderSource` 枚举 |

| FR-ORDER-052 | 产品规格摘要（cpSummary） | `ProductController::getPrice` / `OrderController::create` | `POST /api/Product/GetPrice` | `orders.cp_summary` |
| FR-ORDER-056 | 配送方式枚举 | `OrderController::create` | `POST /api/Order/Create` | `DeliveryType` 枚举 |
| FR-ORDER-057 | 取消原因枚举 | `OrderController::cancel` | `POST /api/Order/Cancel` | `orders.cancel_reason`（0~9） |

## 3. 模块六：支付系统（FR-PAY-022, 025~027, 029）

> **审查结论**：FR-PAY-022（预存款充值）、FR-PAY-025~027（支付密码）、FR-PAY-029（多级定金）代码已存在但SDD未映射。本节补全完整设计。

---

### 3.1 预存款充值（FR-PAY-022）

```php
<?php

// app/Domains/Payment/Actions/RechargePreDepositAction.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Payment\Actions;

use App\Models\CustomerAccount;
use App\Models\PreDepositTransaction;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\DB;

/**
 * 预存款充值Action
 * FR-PAY-022
 */
class RechargePreDepositAction
{
    public function __construct(
        private PayGatewayService $gatewayService,
    ) {}

    public function execute(int $customerId, float $amount, string $payChannel, ?string $remark = null): array
    {
        return DB::transaction(function () use ($customerId, $amount, $payChannel, $remark) {
            // 创建充值流水（待支付状态）
            $transaction = PreDepositTransaction::create([
                'customer_id'   => $customerId,
                'type'          => 'recharge',
                'amount'        => $amount,
                'pay_channel'   => $payChannel,
                'status'        => 'pending',
                'remark'        => $remark,
                'transaction_no'=> 'RCG' . date('Ymd') . strtoupper(uniqid()),
            ]);

            // 申请支付链接
            $payResult = $this->gatewayService->createPayOrder(
                orderNo: $transaction->transaction_no,
                amount: $amount,
                subject: '预存款充值',
                body: "充值金额：{$amount}元",
                channel: $payChannel,
            );

            return [
                'transaction_no' => $transaction->transaction_no,
                'pay_url'        => $payResult['pay_url'],
                'pay_params'     => $payResult['pay_params'],
                'amount'         => $amount,
                'expire_at'      => $payResult['expire_at'],
            ];
        });
    }

    /**
     * 充值到账回调处理
     */
    public function confirmRecharge(string $transactionNo, array $notifyData): void
    {
        DB::transaction(function () use ($transactionNo, $notifyData) {
            $transaction = PreDepositTransaction::where('transaction_no', $transactionNo)
                ->where('status', 'pending')
                ->lockForUpdate()
                ->firstOrFail();

            // 更新流水状态
            $transaction->status = 'success';
            $transaction->paid_at = now();
            $transaction->notify_data = $notifyData;
            $transaction->save();

            // 更新客户账户余额
            $account = CustomerAccount::firstOrCreate(
                ['customer_id' => $transaction->customer_id],
                ['balance' => 0, 'total_recharge' => 0]
            );

            $account->balance += $transaction->amount;
            $account->total_recharge += $transaction->amount;
            $account->save();
        });
    }
}
```

**Controller 方法扩展：**

```php
<?php

// 在 PayController 中补充/显式映射：

use App\Domains\Payment\Actions\RechargePreDepositAction;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\RechargePreDepositRequest;

class PayController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        // ... 已有依赖 ...
        private RechargePreDepositAction $rechargeAction,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 预存款充值
     * FR-PAY-022
     * POST /api/Customer/UpdateAccountPreDeposit
     */
    public function recharge(RechargePreDepositRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->rechargeAction->execute(
            customerId: auth('sanctum')->id(),
            amount: $request->input('amount'),
            payChannel: $request->input('pay_channel', 'wechat'),
            remark: $request->input('remark'),
        );

        return $this->success($result);
    }
}
```

### 3.2 支付密码（FR-PAY-025~027）

```php
<?php

// app/Domains/Payment/Services/PayPasswordService.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Payment\Services;

use App\Models\Customer;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Hash;

/**
 * 支付密码服务
 * FR-PAY-025 ~ FR-PAY-028
 */
class PayPasswordService
{
    /**
     * FR-PAY-025: 设置/修改支付密码
     */
    public function setPassword(int $customerId, string $password, ?string $oldPassword = null): void
    {
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);

        // 修改时需校验旧密码
        if ($customer->pay_password && $oldPassword !== null) {
            if (!Hash::check($oldPassword, $customer->pay_password)) {
                throw new \RuntimeException('原支付密码错误');
            }
        }

        // 密码强度校验
        $this->validateStrength($password);

        $customer->pay_password = Hash::make($password);
        $customer->pay_password_set_at = now();
        $customer->pay_password_error_count = 0;
        $customer->save();
    }

    /**
     * FR-PAY-026: 校验支付密码接口
     */
    public function verifyPassword(int $customerId, string $password): bool
    {
        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);

        if (empty($customer->pay_password)) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('未设置支付密码');
        }

        // FR-PAY-028: 安全策略——错误次数锁定
        if ($customer->pay_password_error_count >= 5) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('支付密码已锁定，请通过找回功能重置');
        }

        if (!Hash::check($password, $customer->pay_password)) {
            $customer->increment('pay_password_error_count');
            throw new \RuntimeException('支付密码错误');
        }

        // 校验成功，清零错误次数
        if ($customer->pay_password_error_count > 0) {
            $customer->pay_password_error_count = 0;
            $customer->save();
        }

        return true;
    }

    /**
     * FR-PAY-027: 支付密码找回（通过短信验证码重置）
     */
    public function resetPassword(int $customerId, string $smsCode, string $newPassword): void
    {
        // 校验短信验证码（复用 SmsService）
        $smsService = app(SmsService::class);
        if (!$smsService->verifyCode($customerId, $smsCode, 'pay_password_reset')) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('短信验证码错误');
        }

        $this->validateStrength($newPassword);

        $customer = Customer::findOrFail($customerId);
        $customer->pay_password = Hash::make($newPassword);
        $customer->pay_password_set_at = now();
        $customer->pay_password_error_count = 0;
        $customer->save();
    }

    /**
     * 密码强度校验
     */
    private function validateStrength(string $password): void
    {
        if (strlen($password) < 6 || strlen($password) > 20) {
            throw new \InvalidArgumentException('支付密码长度应为6-20位');
        }
        if (!preg_match('/^\d+$/', $password)) {
            throw new \InvalidArgumentException('支付密码必须为纯数字');
        }
    }
}
```

**Controller 方法扩展：**

```php
<?php

// 在 PayController 中补充/显式映射：

use App\Domains\Payment\Services\PayPasswordService;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\ResetPayPasswordRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\SetPayPasswordRequest;
use App\Http\Requests\Pay\VerifyPayPasswordRequest;

class PayController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        // ... 已有依赖 ...
        private PayPasswordService $payPasswordService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * FR-PAY-025: 设置/修改支付密码
     * POST /api/Pay/SetPayPassword
     */
    public function setPayPassword(SetPayPasswordRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->payPasswordService->setPassword(
            customerId: auth('sanctum')->id(),
            password: $request->input('password'),
            oldPassword: $request->input('old_password'),
        );

        return $this->success(['message' => '支付密码设置成功']);
    }

    /**
     * FR-PAY-026: 校验支付密码
     * POST /api/Pay/VerifyPayPassword
     */
    public function verifyPayPassword(VerifyPayPasswordRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $result = $this->payPasswordService->verifyPassword(
            customerId: auth('sanctum')->id(),
            password: $request->input('password'),
        );

        return $this->success(['valid' => $result]);
    }

    /**
     * FR-PAY-027: 支付密码找回
     * POST /api/Pay/ResetPayPassword
     */
    public function resetPayPassword(ResetPayPasswordRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $this->payPasswordService->resetPassword(
            customerId: auth('sanctum')->id(),
            smsCode: $request->input('sms_code'),
            newPassword: $request->input('new_password'),
        );

        return $this->success(['message' => '支付密码重置成功']);
    }
}
```

### 3.3 多级定金（FR-PAY-029 / FR-ORDER-035~038）

```php
<?php

// app/Domains/Payment/Services/DepositPaymentService.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Domains\Payment\Services;

use App\Enums\DepositPhase;
use App\Enums\OrderSign;
use App\Models\Order;

/**
 * 多级定金支付服务
 * FR-PAY-029: 支持 unPaidDeposit0/1/2/6/7 多级定金阶段控制
 */
class DepositPaymentService
{
    public function __construct(
        private PayGatewayService $gatewayService,
        private OrderStatusTransitionService $orderTransitionService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * 根据当前定金阶段计算应付金额
     */
    public function calculatePayableAmount(Order $order): float
    {
        $phase = DepositPhase::from($order->deposit_phase);

        return match ($phase) {
            DepositPhase::PHASE_0 => $order->payable_amount, // 全款
            DepositPhase::PHASE_1 => $order->deposit_amount, // 定金
            DepositPhase::PHASE_2 => $order->balance_amount, // 尾款
            DepositPhase::PHASE_6 => $order->deposit_amount, // 特殊定金
            DepositPhase::PHASE_7 => $order->payable_amount, // 账期结算
        };
    }

    /**
     * 支付成功后推进定金阶段
     */
    public function advanceDepositPhase(Order $order): void
    {
        $currentPhase = DepositPhase::from($order->deposit_phase);
        $nextPhase = $currentPhase->next();

        if ($nextPhase === null) {
            // 最终阶段，标记已付尾款
            OrderSign::setFlag($order->order_sign, OrderSign::PAID_BALANCE, true);
            $order->is_paid = true;
            $order->paid_at = now();
        } else {
            $order->deposit_phase = $nextPhase->value;
            if ($currentPhase === DepositPhase::PHASE_0 && $nextPhase === DepositPhase::PHASE_1) {
                OrderSign::setFlag($order->order_sign, OrderSign::PAID_DEPOSIT, true);
            }
        }

        $order->save();
    }

    /**
     * 获取当前阶段收银台配置（显示"付定金"/"付尾款"/"全款"文案）
     */
    public function getCashierConfig(Order $order): array
    {
        $phase = DepositPhase::from($order->deposit_phase);
        $amount = $this->calculatePayableAmount($order);

        return [
            'phase'        => $phase->value,
            'phase_label'  => $phase->label(),
            'amount'       => $amount,
            'total_amount' => $order->payable_amount,
            'paid_amount'  => $order->paid_amount ?? 0,
            'pay_button_text' => match ($phase) {
                DepositPhase::PHASE_0 => '立即支付',
                DepositPhase::PHASE_1 => '支付定金',
                DepositPhase::PHASE_2 => '支付尾款',
                DepositPhase::PHASE_6 => '支付特殊定金',
                DepositPhase::PHASE_7 => '账期结算',
            },
        ];
    }
}
```

### 3.4 FR-PAY 映射汇总

| FR编号 | PRD功能描述 | Controller::Action | API路由 | 关联Service/Action |
|--------|------------|-------------------|---------|-------------------|
| FR-PAY-022 | 预存款充值 | `PayController::recharge` | `POST /api/Customer/UpdateAccountPreDeposit` | `RechargePreDepositAction` |
| FR-PAY-025 | 支付密码设置与修改 | `PayController::setPayPassword` | `POST /api/Pay/SetPayPassword` | `PayPasswordService::setPassword()` |
| FR-PAY-026 | 支付密码校验接口 | `PayController::verifyPayPassword` | `POST /api/Pay/VerifyPayPassword` | `PayPasswordService::verifyPassword()` |
| FR-PAY-027 | 支付密码找回 | `PayController::resetPayPassword` | `POST /api/Pay/ResetPayPassword` | `PayPasswordService::resetPassword()` |
| FR-PAY-028 | 支付密码安全策略 | `PayController::verifyPayPassword` | `POST /api/Pay/VerifyPayPassword` | 错误5次锁定，短信验证码找回 |
| FR-PAY-029 | 多级定金支持 | `PayController::applyPayUrl` | `POST /api/Pay/ApplyPayUrl` | `DepositPaymentService` |

## 4. 模块七：物流与配送（FR-LOG-031, 034, 035）

> **审查结论**：FR-LOG-031（专线轨迹同步）、FR-LOG-034（轨迹展示格式）、FR-LOG-035（签收确认）缺失SDD映射。本节补全完整设计。

---

### 4.1 专线物流自有轨迹同步（FR-LOG-031）

```php
<?php

// app/Jobs/PrivateTrackSyncJob.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Jobs;

use App\Models\OrderDelivery;
use App\Services\PrivateTrackSyncService;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

/**
 * 专线物流轨迹同步Job
 * FR-LOG-031: 对接自有物流系统，定时拉取专线轨迹
 */
class PrivateTrackSyncJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(
        private ?string $orderSn = null, // null 表示全量同步
    ) {}

    public function handle(PrivateTrackSyncService $syncService): void
    {
        if ($this->orderSn) {
            $syncService->syncByOrderSn($this->orderSn);
            return;
        }

        // 全量同步：获取近7天内已发货且未签收的专线订单
        $deliveries = OrderDelivery::where('delivery_type', 0) // 0=专线
            ->where('status', '<', 4) // 未签收
            ->where('shipped_at', '>=', now()->subDays(7))
            ->get();

        foreach ($deliveries as $delivery) {
            try {
                $syncService->syncByDelivery($delivery);
            } catch (\Throwable $e) {
                \Log::error('专线轨迹同步失败', [
                    'order_sn' => $delivery->order_sn,
                    'error'    => $e->getMessage(),
                ]);
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

// app/Services/PrivateTrackSyncService.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Services;

use App\Models\OrderDelivery;
use App\Models\ExpressTrack;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Http;

/**
 * 专线物流轨迹同步服务
 * FR-LOG-031
 */
class PrivateTrackSyncService
{
    private string $apiBaseUrl;
    private string $apiKey;

    public function __construct()
    {
        $this->apiBaseUrl = config('services.private_logistics.api_url');
        $this->apiKey = config('services.private_logistics.api_key');
    }

    public function syncByOrderSn(string $orderSn): void
    {
        $delivery = OrderDelivery::where('order_sn', $orderSn)
            ->where('delivery_type', 0)
            ->firstOrFail();

        $this->syncByDelivery($delivery);
    }

    public function syncByDelivery(OrderDelivery $delivery): void
    {
        $cacheKey = "private_track:{$delivery->order_sn}";

        // 缓存5分钟，避免频繁调用
        if (Cache::has($cacheKey)) {
            return;
        }

        $response = Http::withHeaders([
            'X-API-Key' => $this->apiKey,
        ])->get("{$this->apiBaseUrl}/tracks", [
            'waybill_no' => $delivery->waybill_no,
        ]);

        if (!$response->successful()) {
            throw new \RuntimeException('专线物流接口调用失败：' . $response->body());
        }

        $tracks = $response->json('data.tracks', []);

        foreach ($tracks as $track) {
            ExpressTrack::updateOrCreate(
                [
                    'order_sn'      => $delivery->order_sn,
                    'track_time'    => $track['time'],
                ],
                [
                    'delivery_type' => 0, // 专线
                    'location'      => $track['location'] ?? '',
                    'status'        => $this->mapPrivateStatus($track['status']),
                    'description'   => $track['description'] ?? '',
                    'operator'      => $track['driver_name'] ?? '',
                    'operator_phone'=> $track['driver_phone'] ?? '',
                    'source'        => 'private',
                ]
            );
        }

        Cache::put($cacheKey, true, 300); // 5分钟缓存
    }

    /**
     * 映射专线状态到统一状态码
     */
    private function mapPrivateStatus(string $privateStatus): int
    {
        return match ($privateStatus) {
            'picked_up'  => 1, // 已揽收
            'in_transit' => 2, // 运输中
            'delivering' => 3, // 派送中
            'signed'     => 4, // 已签收
            'exception'  => 5, // 异常
            default      => 0, // 待揽收
        };
    }
}
```

---

### 4.2 轨迹展示格式（FR-LOG-034）

```php
<?php

// app/Http/Resources/ExpressTrackResource.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Resources;

use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\JsonResource;

/**
 * 物流轨迹Resource
 * FR-LOG-034: 返回时间轴格式数据（时间、地点、状态、操作员）
 */
class ExpressTrackResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'id'             => $this->id,
            'order_sn'       => $this->order_sn,
            'track_time'     => $this->track_time,
            'location'       => $this->location,
            'status'         => $this->status,
            'status_label'   => $this->getStatusLabel((int) $this->status),
            'description'    => $this->description,
            'operator'       => $this->operator,
            'operator_phone' => $this->operator_phone,
            'source'         => $this->source, // 'express' / 'private'
            'created_at'     => $this->created_at?->toDateTimeString(),
        ];
    }

    private function getStatusLabel(int $status): string
    {
        return match ($status) {
            0 => '待揽收',
            1 => '已揽收',
            2 => '运输中',
            3 => '派送中',
            4 => '已签收',
            5 => '异常',
            6 => '已退回',
            default => '未知',
        };
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

// app/Http/Resources/ExpressTrackTimelineResource.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Resources;

use Illuminate\Http\Request;
use Illuminate\Http\Resources\Json\JsonResource;

/**
 * 物流轨迹时间轴Resource
 * FR-LOG-034: 按日期分组的时间轴展示
 */
class ExpressTrackTimelineResource extends JsonResource
{
    public function toArray(Request $request): array
    {
        return [
            'order_sn'       => $this['order_sn'],
            'express_company'=> $this['express_company'] ?? '',
            'express_no'     => $this['express_no'] ?? '',
            'delivery_type'  => $this['delivery_type'] ?? 1,
            'delivery_type_label' => $this->getDeliveryTypeLabel($this['delivery_type'] ?? 1),
            'current_status' => $this['current_status'],
            'timeline'       => $this['timeline'], // 按日期分组的时间轴
            'is_signed'      => $this['is_signed'] ?? false,
            'signed_at'      => $this['signed_at'] ?? null,
        ];
    }

    private function getDeliveryTypeLabel(int $type): string
    {
        return match ($type) {
            0 => '专线物流',
            1 => '快递',
            2 => '云仓',
            3 => '门店自提',
            default => '未知',
        };
    }
}
```

**Controller 方法扩展：**

```php
<?php

// 在 DeliveryController 中补充：

use App\Http\Resources\ExpressTrackResource;
use App\Http\Resources\ExpressTrackTimelineResource;
use App\Models\ExpressTrack;
use App\Models\OrderDelivery;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Cache;

class DeliveryController extends Controller
{
    /**
     * FR-LOG-034: 物流轨迹查询（时间轴格式）
     * GET /api/Delivery/GetExpressLogsByOrderSN
     */
    public function getExpressLogsByOrderSN(Request $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $orderSn = $request->input('order_sn');

        $tracks = Cache::remember("express_track:{$orderSn}", 3600, function () use ($orderSn) {
            return ExpressTrack::where('order_sn', $orderSn)
                ->orderBy('track_time', 'desc')
                ->get();
        });

        $delivery = OrderDelivery::where('order_sn', $orderSn)->first();

        // 按日期分组构建时间轴
        $timeline = $this->buildTimeline($tracks);

        $data = [
            'order_sn'        => $orderSn,
            'express_company' => $delivery?->express_company,
            'express_no'      => $delivery?->waybill_no,
            'delivery_type'   => $delivery?->delivery_type ?? 1,
            'current_status'  => $tracks->first()?->status ?? 0,
            'timeline'        => $timeline,
            'is_signed'       => $tracks->contains('status', 4),
            'signed_at'       => $tracks->firstWhere('status', 4)?->track_time,
        ];

        return $this->success(new ExpressTrackTimelineResource($data));
    }

    private function buildTimeline($tracks): array
    {
        $grouped = $tracks->groupBy(function ($track) {
            return substr($track->track_time, 0, 10); // 按日期 YYYY-MM-DD 分组
        });

        $timeline = [];
        foreach ($grouped as $date => $dayTracks) {
            $timeline[] = [
                'date'   => $date,
                'tracks' => ExpressTrackResource::collection($dayTracks),
            ];
        }

        return $timeline;
    }
}
```

---

### 4.3 签收确认（FR-LOG-035）

```php
<?php

// app/Jobs/GenerateThumbnailJob.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Jobs;

use App\Models\OrderFile;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Storage;
use Intervention\Image\ImageManager;

class GenerateThumbnailJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public function __construct(private int $orderFileId) {}

    public function handle(ImageManager $imageManager): void
    {
        $orderFile = OrderFile::find($this->orderFileId);
        if (! $orderFile || ! Storage::exists($orderFile->file_path)) {
            return;
        }

        $filePath = $orderFile->file_path;
        $thumbPath = dirname($filePath) . '/' . pathinfo($filePath, PATHINFO_FILENAME) . '_thumb.' . pathinfo($filePath, PATHINFO_EXTENSION);

        try {
            $image = $imageManager->read(Storage::path($filePath));
            $image->scaleDown(width: 300);
            $image->save(Storage::path($thumbPath));

            $orderFile->update(['thumb_url' => Storage::url($thumbPath)]);
        } catch (\Throwable $e) {
            \Log::warning('缩略图生成失败', [
                'order_file_id' => $this->orderFileId,
                'error' => $e->getMessage(),
            ]);
        }
    }
}

```

```php
<?php

// app/Jobs/AutoConfirmReceiveJob.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Jobs;

use App\Models\Order;
use App\Services\OrderStatusTransitionService;
use Illuminate\Bus\Queueable;
use Illuminate\Contracts\Queue\ShouldQueue;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Bus\Dispatchable;
use Illuminate\Queue\InteractsWithQueue;
use Illuminate\Queue\SerializesModels;

/**
 * 7天自动签收Job
 * FR-LOG-035: 超7天未手动确认，自动标记已完成
 */
class AutoConfirmReceiveJob implements ShouldQueue
{
    use Dispatchable, InteractsWithQueue, Queueable, SerializesModels;

    public function handle(OrderStatusTransitionService $transitionService): void
    {
        $orders = Order::where('status', 5) // 已发货
            ->where('shipped_at', '<=', now()->subDays(7))
            ->whereNull('completed_at')
            ->get();

        foreach ($orders as $order) {
            try {
                $transitionService->toCompleted($order, autoConfirm: true);
            } catch (\Throwable $e) {
                \Log::error('自动签收失败', [
                    'order_sn' => $order->order_sn,
                    'error'    => $e->getMessage(),
                ]);
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```php
<?php

// app/Http/Requests/Order/ConfirmReceiveRequest.php
declare(strict_types=1);

namespace App\Http\Requests\Order;

use Illuminate\Foundation\Http\FormRequest;

class ConfirmReceiveRequest extends FormRequest
{
    public function authorize(): bool
    {
        return auth('sanctum')->check();
    }

    public function rules(): array
    {
        return [
            'order_sn'      => ['required', 'string', 'exists:orders,order_sn'],
            'sign_image'    => ['nullable', 'string'], // 电子签名图片URL（可选）
            'sign_type'     => ['nullable', 'in:manual,auto,electronic'], // 签收类型
        ];
    }
}
```

**Controller 方法扩展：**

```php
<?php

// 在 OrderController 中补充/显式映射：

use App\Http\Requests\Order\ConfirmReceiveRequest;
use App\Services\OrderStatusTransitionService;

class OrderController extends Controller
{
    public function __construct(
        // ... 已有依赖 ...
        private OrderStatusTransitionService $transitionService,
    ) {}

    /**
     * FR-LOG-035 / FR-ORDER-029: 确认收货/签收
     * POST /api/Order/ConfirmReceive
     */
    public function confirmReceive(ConfirmReceiveRequest $request): JsonResponse
    {
        $order = Order::where('order_sn', $request->input('order_sn'))
            ->where('customer_id', auth('sanctum')->id())
            ->firstOrFail();

        $this->transitionService->toCompleted($order, autoConfirm: false);

        // 可选：保存电子签名
        if ($request->has('sign_image')) {
            $order->sign_image = $request->input('sign_image');
            $order->sign_type = $request->input('sign_type', 'electronic');
            $order->save();
        }

        return $this->success(['message' => '确认收货成功']);
    }
}
```

### 4.4 调度配置

```php
<?php

// routes/console.php 或 app/Console/Kernel.php

use App\Jobs\AutoConfirmReceiveJob;
use App\Jobs\PrivateTrackSyncJob;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schedule;

// 专线轨迹同步：每15分钟执行一次
Schedule::job(new PrivateTrackSyncJob())->everyFifteenMinutes();

// 快递轨迹同步（已存在，补充对比）
Schedule::job(new \App\Jobs\SyncExpressTracksJob())->everyTenMinutes();

// 7天自动签收：每天凌晨2点执行
Schedule::job(new AutoConfirmReceiveJob())->dailyAt('02:00');
```

### 4.5 FR-LOG 映射汇总

| FR编号 | PRD功能描述 | Controller::Action / Job | API路由 / 调度 | 关联Service/Job |
|--------|------------|------------------------|---------------|----------------|
| FR-LOG-031 | 专线物流自有轨迹 | `PrivateTrackSyncJob::handle()` | 队列定时任务 | `PrivateTrackSyncService` |
| FR-LOG-034 | 轨迹展示格式 | `DeliveryController::getExpressLogsByOrderSN` | `GET /api/Delivery/GetExpressLogsByOrderSN` | `ExpressTrackTimelineResource` |
| FR-LOG-035 | 签收确认 | `OrderController::confirmReceive` / `AutoConfirmReceiveJob` | `POST /api/Order/ConfirmReceive` / 每日02:00 | `OrderStatusTransitionService::toCompleted()` |

### 5.2 数据库迁移扩展

以下字段需通过迁移补充到现有表：

```php
<?php

// database/migrations/xxxx_xx_xx_add_missing_fields_to_orders.php
use Illuminate\Database\Migrations\Migration;
use Illuminate\Database\Schema\Blueprint;
use Illuminate\Support\Facades\Schema;

return new class extends Migration {
    public function up(): void
    {
        Schema::table('orders', function (Blueprint $table) {
            // FR-ORDER-050~058
            $table->string('order_name', 255)->nullable()->comment('订单名称');
            $table->tinyInteger('source')->default(0)->comment('订单来源 WM: 0官网/1小程序/2报价网站');
            $table->integer('create_source')->default(0)->comment('创建来源 lM位掩码');
            $table->string('cp_summary', 500)->nullable()->comment('规格摘要');
            $table->tinyInteger('delivery_type')->default(1)->comment('配送方式: 0专线/1快递/2云仓/3自提');
            $table->tinyInteger('cancel_reason')->nullable()->comment('取消原因 0~9枚举');
            $table->tinyInteger('invoice_status')->default(0)->comment('发票状态');
            $table->integer('order_sign')->default(0)->comment('Sign位掩码 LM');

            // FR-ORDER-035~038, FR-PAY-029
            $table->decimal('deposit_amount', 12, 2)->default(0)->comment('定金金额');
            $table->decimal('balance_amount', 12, 2)->default(0)->comment('尾款金额');

            // FR-ORDER-021~033 状态流转相关
            $table->tinyInteger('modify_status')->default(0)->comment('修改状态');
            $table->text('modify_content')->nullable()->comment('修改内容');
            $table->timestamp('modify_applied_at')->nullable();
            $table->timestamp('modify_confirmed_at')->nullable();
            $table->tinyInteger('refund_status')->default(0)->comment('退款状态');
            $table->decimal('refund_amount', 12, 2)->default(0)->comment('退款金额');
            $table->string('refund_reason', 500)->nullable();
            $table->tinyInteger('original_status')->nullable()->comment('退款/售后前的原始FM状态');
            $table->timestamp('cancelled_at')->nullable();
            $table->timestamp('shipped_at')->nullable();
            $table->timestamp('completed_at')->nullable();
            $table->boolean('is_auto_confirmed')->default(false)->comment('是否自动确认');
            // 注：sign_image / sign_type 已迁移至 order_deliveries / order_multi_deliveries 表
        });

        Schema::create('order_modify_histories', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id();
            $table->foreignId('order_id')->constrained()->onDelete('cascade');
            $table->text('content')->comment('修改内容');
            $table->tinyInteger('modify_type')->default(0)->comment('修改类型：0-金额修改 1-地址修改 2-规格修改');
            $table->decimal('before_amount', 12, 2)->nullable()->comment('修改前订单金额');
            $table->decimal('after_amount', 12, 2)->nullable()->comment('修改后订单金额');
            $table->foreignId('applied_by')->nullable()->comment('修改申请人');
            $table->foreignId('confirmed_by')->nullable()->comment('修改确认人');
            $table->timestamp('confirmed_at')->nullable()->comment('修改确认时间');
            $table->tinyInteger('status')->default(0)->comment('修改记录状态：0-待确认 1-已确认 2-已拒绝');
            $table->timestamps();
            $table->index('order_id');
            $table->index('status');
        });

        Schema::create('order_status_histories', function (Blueprint $table) {
            $table->id();
            $table->foreignId('order_id')->constrained()->onDelete('cascade');
            $table->tinyInteger('from_status')->comment('原状态');
            $table->tinyInteger('to_status')->comment('目标状态');
            $table->string('remark', 500)->nullable();
            $table->foreignId('operator_id')->nullable();
            $table->string('operator_type', 20)->nullable()->comment('操作者类型');
            $table->timestamps();
            $table->index('order_id');
        });
    }
};
```

## VIP模块（FR-VIP-001~018）

> **综述**：本模块18个FR中，FR-VIP-001~009的VIP等级/成长值/权益/截稿时间设计映射在 `supplement_vip_level_full.md` 中补充；FR-VIP-010~018的优惠券与促销设计映射在SDD主文档6.43节中覆盖。

| FR编号 | 功能描述 | SDD位置 | 代码元素 | 状态 |
